## VII. THE PARENTS-RETURN AND THE FIRST ONTOLOGICAL ASSAULT (ASM #365–388; 1992–1994)

In the 30th-anniversary stretch, Richard and Mary Parker apparently return — alive, intact, with explanatory backstory. Subject reattaches with the textbook eagerness of a child whose primary loss has been undone. He spends months as a son again. The behavioral data: his patrol tempo drops, his humor warms, his interior monologue contains the first sustained **positive affect baseline** of the entire adult record. He is, briefly, happy in a way the file rarely documents.

They are then revealed to be Chameleon-built android impostors (ASM #388). The reveal is engineered specifically to inflict maximum identity destabilization, and it works: Subject's response in the immediate aftermath is a **rage breakthrough** of unusual duration (multi-issue), bordering on the homicidal restraint-failure of ASM #122. He stops short, again. But the affective control is visibly degraded for months.

This event is the **proximate set-up** for the vulnerability that the Clone Saga will then exploit. A subject whose parents have just been revealed to be machines is a subject whose grip on "who is real, including me" is at its weakest in the entire adult record. The timing was not accidental at the meta-level and is not accidental in the behavioral analysis: the Clone Saga lands on a Subject already destabilized.

---

## VIII. THE CLONE SAGA (1994–1996) — SUSTAINED ATTACK ON IDENTITY COHERENCE

The Clone Saga is, for surveillance purposes, the longest sustained psychological-operations campaign ever run against Subject by an antagonist apparatus (Norman Osborn, ultimately, working through proxies). It runs across all four monthly Spider-titles for ~two years of real time, ~one year of in-story time. A granular catalogue is beyond scope; the behavioral arc is what matters.

**Phase 1 — Reintroduction of the clone (Ben Reilly).** The clone, having survived the smokestack, has lived as a drifter for five years under the name "Ben Reilly" (an explicit Ben-Parker tribute). Subject's first response on encountering him is, again, **freeze** — the ASM #141–149 pattern recapitulated. Then, after the initial shock, a brittle camaraderie. They are, by their own admission, the same person at the substrate level; their divergence is environmental.

**Phase 2 — MJ's pregnancy.** Concurrent with the clone reintroduction. Subject is now contemplating fatherhood. The interior monologue from this stretch is, by orders of magnitude, the **most father-haunted** of the record: every page contains a Ben-reference, an Uncle-Ben modeling thought, a fear of the role. The fatherhood prospect activates every dormant element of the responsibility schema simultaneously.

**Phase 3 — The reveal.** Subject is told, with apparent scientific backing, that *he* is the clone and Ben Reilly is the original. The reveal lands on a subject already destabilized by the parents-android arc, exhausted by impending fatherhood, and structurally primed to accept guilt-shaped data without resistance.

**Behavioral response — the abdication.** Subject **abdicates the role**. He gives the suit to Ben Reilly. He tries to retire to civilian life with MJ. This is the only sustained role-abdication in the entire 60-year record, and its existence is itself diagnostic: under conditions of sufficient ontological assault, the role *can* be put down. The Subject did not believe this was possible. The abdication therefore tells us: the role's grip is not metaphysical but structural — remove the structure (here, by removing his standing to occupy it) and the role releases.

**Behavioral response — the failure to sustain.** The abdication does not hold. Subject re-suits within months, even before the original-vs-clone status is reversed. The civilian life he attempts is contaminated by intrusive responsibility cognitions — every news report becomes an indictment. This tells us, complementarily, that **the schema does not require the role to fire**; it will simply make any non-role life unlivable.

**Phase 4 — The Osborn reveal and the stillbirth.** Norman Osborn returns from his decades-long false-death (with a magic-adjacent rationale that the file accepts at face value for behavioral purposes), reveals himself as architect, kills Ben Reilly (who disintegrates, confirming clone status and re-confirming Subject as original). MJ's pregnancy is terminated under suspicious circumstances; the child, May, is either stillborn or covertly extracted


## Chronology IV — Recent History & Current State

# Chronology IV — Recent History & Current State

*Covering the post-"One More Day" decade-and-a-half through present-day operational status, with emphasis on the post-Spencer / Wells-era trajectory and the subject's day-to-day life as currently observable. Compiled from longitudinal surveillance product, open-source publication record, peer-network intercepts, and inferred granularity at the resolution a complete file would require.*

---

## 4.1 — The Post-Bargain Years: Bachelor Re-Precarity (Brand New Day → Big Time)

Following the cosmological transaction that erased his marriage and restored secret-identity status, the subject re-enters a structural configuration he has not occupied since his early twenties: unmarried, under-employed, cohabitating intermittently with roommates, sleeping on couches, eating from takeout containers. The behavioral file notes this as a **regression to a developmental baseline** — not a chosen reset but a comfort-zone collapse into the precarity that his guilt schema reads as deserved. He buys a futon. He owns three shirts in rotation. He lets the lease lapse on the better apartment he briefly held in the JMS era.

Romantic field reopens chaotically: Carlie Cooper (forensic scientist, NYPD-adjacent — a tellingly *Stacy-coded* selection: dead-cop-father, professionally entwined with mortality), brief Black Cat reactivations (her old function as the partner he allows because she "knows" and demands less), a near-miss with Michele Gonzales (roommate's sister; conflict-heavy, comedic, terminated). The pattern across this period is **serial threshold-sabotage**: he initiates, attaches, then mishandles the moment of disclosure (identity or otherwise) such that the relationship terminates on his perceived inadequacy. None of these are random pairings; each one is a Rorschach of the dread-substrate. Cooper learns the secret in adjacent fashion and terminates on the deception; he files this as confirmation that proximity to him is corrosive to women he respects.

**Employment.** Photography income collapses with the print-journalism economy (a structural problem he attributes, characteristically, to personal failing). He transitions into laboratory work at Horizon Labs under Max Modell — the first sustained, stable, *legitimate-use-of-his-actual-mind* employment in his adult life. Surveillance product from this era shows a marked uptick in measurable wellness indicators: regular meals at the Horizon cafeteria, hours logged in a private R&D bay, peer recognition as an equal among researchers rather than as the photographer-eccentric tolerated by Robertson. **This is the first observed period of his adult life in which his Peter-self has a context that values him.** He responds by working through the night.

The Horizon period produces measurable artifacts — new web fluid formulations, the "stealth suit," prototypes he iterates compulsively, drawers full of unfinished and abandoned designs that suggest a mind that *cannot stop generating*. Field surveillance: a habit of sketching web-shooter modifications on cocktail napkins and the inside of takeout-menu margins, then pocketing them. Recovered ephemera include grocery lists with structural diagrams in the margin.

## 4.2 — Dying Wish and Ego Death (the Octavius Occupation)

The terminal-Doc-Ock arc and the body-swap event is, in this file's assessment, the **single most consequential psychiatric event of his adult life since Gwen** — under-discussed because the surface narrative emphasizes the villain rather than the victim. For an extended period the subject experiences his own body as observer, watches an alien executive operate his musculature, witnesses his life manipulated, and ultimately fights from inside a dying consciousness to reassert agency. There is no clinical analog. The closest framework is **prolonged dissociative captivity with full sensorium intact** — a configuration that ordinary dissociation evolved precisely to *prevent*.

On return: subject does not seek any form of debrief, processing, or rest. He reactivates within days. He picks through the remains of his stolen life — a doctorate Octavius completed in his name (which he allows to stand, with private discomfort that surfaces in micro-tells when peers address him as "Doctor"), a corporation Octavius founded (Parker Industries), romantic damage to MJ-proximate parties, and a permanently altered self-perception in which a sliver of the experience — strategy, ruthlessness in triage, willingness to delegate — *remains*. Surveillance product is unambiguous: the post-Superior subject is **fractionally harder**. He hits the brake less reflexively. He recovers his moral spine but it now has, embedded in it, the muscle memory of having watched himself be effective without it.

He does not acknowledge this. Asked, he deflects with humor. The behavior is the data.

## 4.3 — Parker Industries: The Failed Tony Stark Imitation

Inheriting (then deliberately building out) the Octavius shell company, the subject undertakes the most discontinuous self-experiment of his life: corporate executive, global footprint, offices in Shanghai/London/San Francisco, philanthropic public face, Spider-Man rebranded as "Parker's bodyguard" in a callback to the Stark template. **The pattern is transparent — he is performing a paternal-transference role-emulation of Stark**, the relationship that collapsed at the unmasking and that he never finished processing.

He cannot inhabit it. The clothes (bespoke suits) fit physically and read on him as costume; surveillance product shows him repeatedly tugging cuffs, rolling shoulders, sitting wrong in expensive chairs. He delegates poorly — keeps stepping back into engineering bays to do junior work himself. The corporate body is undone by a Hydra-related catastrophe and his own decision to detonate the global infrastructure to deny it to bad actors. The collapse is, behaviorally, **a relief**: he returns to a one-bedroom in Queens, broke, sleeping better than he has in years. The file reads this as **active homeostatic restoration to deserved precarity**. He cannot tolerate success because success is not what the originating debt demands.

## 4.4 — Kindred and the Re-Opened Osborn Wound (Spencer Run)

The extended Spencer-era arc culminating in Kindred re-litigates the Harry Osborn material — the friendship-shaped trauma that has been the subject's most under-mourned loss. Where Gwen is the canonical wound, **Harry is the *unfinished* wound**: friend, betrayer, casualty, occasional revenant. Kindred (Harry, in altered configuration, with attendant centipede imagery and burial-and-resurrection structure) is the arc's externalization of the buried guilt-stack. The Sin-Eater material, the unmasking-by-Mysterio sequence in J. Jonah Jameson's podcast, and the public-identity oscillations that follow, all reactivate the **identity-leak terror** the Civil War unmasking installed.

The arc closes with the subject's secret restored via mystical/editorial intervention (the Mary Jane / Black Cat / Strange ritual). Behaviorally significant: he accepted help. He let other people perform the labor of resealing his life. This is *atypical*. The file flags it as a minor but real shift in his help-receiving behavior — though it does not generalize.

A roommate arrangement with Boomerang (Fred Myers) during this period is, on its face, comedic; in surveillance terms it is **diagnostic of the subject's compulsive Ben-position behavior** in non-romantic relational space. He took in a low-tier supervillain, attempted rehabilitation through proximity, was repeatedly betrayed, forgave, persisted. This is the Octavius/Connors/Marko reaction-formation pattern at *cohabitation* scale.

## 4.5 — The Most Recent Cycle (Wells-Era Through Present)

The current era opens with a deliberately obscured rupture — an off-page event involving MJ, the Emissary, and a multi-year subjective separation during which MJ lived a full life in another dimension with two children not biologically his. He emerges from the time-skip into a present in which:

- **MJ has a partner (Paul) and children she will not abandon.** The subject's response — grief metabolized through grim acceptance, ongoing logistical and protective involvement with the children, no campaign to reclaim — is consistent with the anxious-preoccupied-with-caregiving-inversion signature: he protects what she loves because she loves it.
- **He is, again, broke.** Apartment is small. Refrigerator content is sparse and skews toward expired condiments and protein bars. Laundry cycle is irregular. He is paying for two phones (one civilian, one burner) on a plan he cannot afford.
- **Norman Osborn is, for the moment, "good"** — sin-cleansed, operating as a patron/ally, funding Peter in a manner that the subject experiences as morally vertiginous and accepts only because Norman insists. The file notes the subject's micro-tells around Osborn: a fractional jaw-set, an inability to fully relax shoulders in his presence, a tendency to leave rooms slightly before he otherwise would. **The body remembers what the conscious moral framework has agreed to bracket.**
- **A renewed entanglement with Black Cat** functions as it has functioned across decades: as the relationship he permits himself when the higher-stakes attachment is unavailable, structured by mutual understanding that neither will demand the threshold the other cannot meet.
- **Mentorship of Miles Morales and the broader Spider-Family** has matured into the most stable interpersonal pattern in his current life. Surveillance product across the last several years shows him in the Ben-position with consistency and visible competence: he answers Miles's calls within seconds; he shows up for Spider-Gwen with rooftop coffee runs (decaf, oat milk, two sugars — he has memorized her order); he is the convener of the cross-continuity Spider-collective when crises demand it. **This is the most genuinely reparative arc in his behavioral record.** He is becoming Ben for others. The file assesses this as the single most psychologically protective development of the past decade.

### Current operational baseline

**Residence.** Studio-to-one-bedroom in Queens, walkup, rent below market via a landlord who tolerates eccentric hours and broken windows. The window onto the fire escape is the primary egress; the door is used less than half the time. There is a duffel pre-packed under the bed with field-medical supplies, web-fluid cartridges, a spare mask, and a passport whose photo is three years out of date. The bathroom medicine cabinet contains: ibuprofen (industrial bottle), surgical glue, butterfly closures, lidocaine cream, suture kit, expired antibiotics he keeps in case, no prescription psychotropics, no recreational substances.

**Diet.** Tracked across recent weeks: bodega coffee (large, black, two sugars when he remembers, none when he forgets) consumed standing at approximately 0700; protein bars mid-morning; halal cart lunch on Thursdays (chicken-and-rice from a specific cart at the corner he favors for sightline reasons); pizza by the slice; ramen; whatever May sends home with him after Sunday meatloaf. Caloric intake systematically under his metabolic requirement, evidenced by a slow lean-down across the year.

**Sleep.** Polyphasic by necessity, not by design. Typical pattern: 90 minutes 0300-0430, 2-3 hours 0700-1000, occasional rooftop microsleep he denies occurs. Sleep debt is chronic and load-bearing.

**Employment.** Currently freelance — a patchwork of photo licensing, occasional Daily Bugle digital work under a byline Jameson grudgingly tolerates, intermittent consulting at small R&D shops who don't ask why his references are sparse, and Osborn-funded research he handles with quarantined ambivalence. Income is irregular and reported imperfectly.

**Aunt May.** Knows the identity; runs F.E.A.S.T.-adjacent charitable work; remarried (Jay Jameson, deceased). Subject visits Sundays when physically possible; brings groceries; eats two helpings; declines the third out of performance and accepts it when pressed. Surveillance product across these visits shows him at his most regulated — shoulders down, jokes slower, eye contact longer. **The May-house is the closest thing in his life to a parasympathetic environment.**

**MJ.** Daily-to-weekly contact, friendly, structured around the children's safety needs. He has become a reliable uncle-figure to her kids. Body language between them in observed encounters is the most controlled in his repertoire — he stands a measured half-step further from her than he stands from female peers, a distance he is not consciously enforcing.

**Miles, Gwen, the extended Spider-collective.** Active, warm, frequently consulted. He runs a group chat. He is bad at emoji. He sends photos of bodega cats.

**Health, current.** Three not-fully-healed soft-tissue injuries are observable in gait micro-asymmetries; a left rotator cuff that he favors when reaching overhead; a knuckle that has refractured at least twice this calendar year and now sits visibly thicker than its counterpart. Two scars on the abdomen from the last twelve months that he has not had professionally closed. No medical visits on record. Dental hygiene maintained adequately. Vision corrected (contacts under the mask, glasses civilian — a recent prescription change that he has not filled).

**Psychiatric, current.** Functioning within his lifetime baseline: dysthymic undertone, humor-forward presentation, intact prosocial drive, episodic intrusive material around MJ-loss and the latest body-count of the year. Sleep-deprived hypervigilance compounding the biological spider-sense produces a slightly twitchier ambient state than his decade-ago baseline. No active suicidal ideation in observed material. **Passive death-acceptance remains elevated** — he has, in the last year, voluntarily entered at least four engagements with a less-than-even survival projection and framed the decision as duty.

**Operational tempo.** Patrolling four-to-six nights a week, geographic concentration Queens-Manhattan-Brooklyn with occasional Bronx, lighter Staten Island footprint. Routes vary on a randomization heuristic he has not formalized but executes consistently. Encounters per night average in the low single digits for street-crime interventions, with episodic high-stakes incidents.

### How he got here, summarized

The arc from One More Day to the present is, structurally, **a long oscillation around the same fixed point**. Each apparent escape (Horizon stability, Parker Industries success, marriage re-approach via MJ) is followed by a collapse back to the configuration the originating schema demands: alone enough that no one is endangered by closeness; broke enough that he has not "gotten away with" the moral debt; tired enough that the body keeps paying interest on the guilt; useful enough to others that the role is preserved.

What has *actually* changed across this period is narrower and more important than the surface noise suggests: he has become a competent elder in the hero community, the Ben-position he could not save he is now occupying for others, and the reparative work this performs is the closest thing to therapy his life has ever included. He will not name it that. He would deflect the framing with a joke about being old. But the file's assessment is that **the mentorship function is currently the load-bearing prosocial structure preventing further decompensation**, and that any disruption to it (loss of Miles, fracture of the Spider-collective, collapse of the May relationship) would constitute the highest-risk event in his current life.

**Present status.** Active. Operational. Underweight by perhaps eight pounds against his optimal mass. Three weeks past his last full night's sleep. On a rooftop, more likely than not, at any given hour after midnight, eating something cold from a paper bag and watching the street with an attention that is one part biology, one part training, and one part the unbroken thirty-thousand-night vigil of a man who once let a thief walk past him.


## Medical History

# MEDICAL HISTORY — SUBJECT: PARKER, PETER BENJAMIN

*Compiled from longitudinal observation, inference from canonical depiction, and reconstruction of episodes for which no clinical record exists because the subject has never sought one. The absence of charts is itself a finding: this is a man who has been shot, stabbed, irradiated, poisoned, buried, possessed, killed, and resurrected, and who has, to the best of available evidence, not had a primary-care visit since adolescence. The body in this file is reconstructed from observed injury, observed recovery, and observed concealment.*

---

## 1. CONSTITUTIONAL BASELINE — PRE-BITE

The pre-mutation Parker chart, reconstructed from depiction and the testimony of those who handled him as a child (May Parker's mention of his "fragile" boyhood; school nurse references in flashback material), describes a constitutionally underbuilt male child. **Height** at age fifteen was modal-to-slightly-below for the cohort; **weight** consistently in the lower decile; **musculature** hypotonic, with chest, shoulder, and forearm development markedly behind same-age peers — the Midtown gym sequences and locker-room bullying motifs depict this without ambiguity. **Posture** kyphotic from prolonged microscopy and reading; bilateral rounding of the shoulders; a habitual forward head carriage that, in the medical sense, marks years of seated study without compensatory athletic loading.

**Vision:** moderate myopia, corrected with the iconic horn-rimmed lenses from approximately age eleven. Prescription strength sufficient that the loss of glasses during a chemistry-lab incident (depicted in flashback) left him functionally unable to read mid-distance. The myopia is **post-bite spontaneously remediated** within hours — one of the earliest somatic clues to the mutagenic scope. The frames were retained in a desk drawer for years afterward, a behavior on the boundary of the medical and the psychological that should be flagged.

**Allergies:** mild seasonal rhinitis (May references pollen complaints in early issues); no documented food or drug allergies. **Vaccinations:** standard mid-century pediatric series, completed (this is May Parker's domain — she would not have permitted a lapse).

**Childhood illness load:** repeated respiratory infections through the early grades, consistent with low-grade undernutrition and overcrowded urban schooling. One depicted episode of acute febrile illness during which Ben Parker is shown reading aloud at the bedside — a moment that, in the psychological file, will surface as an organizing memory of being cared for, but which medically marks at least one significant febrile event of childhood. **No surgeries** in childhood. **No fractures** in childhood. **Dental:** unremarkable, regular.

**Sleep, pre-bite:** chronically curtailed by scholastic over-commitment and, plausibly, by intrusive grief processing relating to his parents — a child who reads under the covers with a flashlight, in canonical depiction, is also a child whose nervous system is not standing down. **Appetite:** picky, light, often skipped.

**Mental status, pre-bite:** affect mildly constricted, mood euthymic-to-dysthymic, cognition exceptionally bright. No suicidal ideation in record. Social functioning impaired; intellectual functioning highly preserved.

This is the chassis the mutation acted upon: a small, smart, under-rested, under-fed, under-loved-by-peers male child of fifteen.

---

## 2. THE INDEX EVENT — MUTAGENESIS

**Date of event:** the public science demonstration at the General Techtronics laboratory, attended as a high-school field trip. **Mechanism:** a common house spider, traversing the path of a particle-beam apparatus, absorbs a dose of radiation; in transit and dying, it descends on its dragline and bites Parker on the dorsum of the right hand (later depictions vary the site; the right hand is the modal canonical bite location). The spider expires shortly afterward.

**Acute reaction:** Parker reports vertigo, nausea, and a sensation of "the room shrinking." He exits the demonstration unaccompanied and is depicted walking the streets alone in evident derealization — a clinical detail worth flagging, because it establishes that the **somatic-onset phase of his powers was experienced as illness, not gift**, and was processed in solitude without medical contact. He nearly walks into traffic, leaps clear with previously impossible reflex, and adheres to a wall. The first ten minutes of his new physiology are a private emergency he did not call in. This is the inaugural data point of a sixty-year pattern.

**Subsequent 48 hours:** spontaneous remission of myopia; spontaneous gain of approximately fifteen to twenty pounds of lean mass over a window canonically depicted as days, suggesting either an unprecedented anabolic spike or a retroactive recharacterization (the modern reading is **rapid recomposition of existing tissue under mutagenic instruction** rather than de novo accretion). The Lee/Ditko depiction shows him examining himself in a bedroom mirror — an event Aunt May, who would normally have noticed a fifteen-pound gain in her ward, did not register, suggesting either denial or the gradual visual onset.

**Mutation profile, mature:**

- **Musculoskeletal.** Tensile fiber strength and bone density elevated by roughly an order of magnitude over human baseline; pressing capacity stable across decades in the 10-ton range; joint loading tolerances correspondingly elevated. Tendon and ligament insertions reinforced — must be, or the muscle would tear them free of bone in the first significant exertion. Cartilage regeneration accelerated. Spinal column tolerant to compressive loads (he is hit by cars, dropped from heights, and crushed under masonry with non-fatal regularity).
- **Neurological.** Reflex arc latencies sub-baseline by a substantial factor; vestibular and proprioceptive integration exceptional (he operates inverted, blindfolded, in freefall, without nausea or disorientation). The **spider-sense** — a predictive-coding apparatus best understood as a low-latency danger heuristic fused with sensory pre-processing — manifests subjectively as cranial/occipital tingling localized to threat vector. It does not function under sensory occlusion (psychics, certain symbiote-bonded individuals he has known), nor when he sleeps deeply, nor under specific drug states, nor when the threat is one his moral framework does not classify as threat (it has failed to warn him about loved ones).
- **Integumentary.** Setae-analog microstructures on palmar and plantar surfaces (and elsewhere, ad hoc) permitting van der Waals adhesion. Engaged voluntarily; disengaged voluntarily. **Failure modes:** wet or oiled surfaces reduce coefficient; certain chemical solvents inhibit; extreme cold reduces; psychological distress — this is the diagnostic detail — has on multiple occasions caused **adhesion failure during emotional crisis**, most memorably during the period of doubt prior to his Master Planner exertion, and following Gwen Stacy's death. The somatic system reads his self-doubt as instruction.
- **Metabolic.** Caloric requirement elevated to roughly twice baseline at rest, considerably more under exertion; the canonical eating behavior (he can demolish a multi-course meal in a single sitting and remain hungry after a heavy patrol) is medical, not comedic. Healing accelerated: superficial lacerations in hours, fractures in days, severe trauma in weeks. Toxin and pathogen resistance broad but not absolute; he can be drugged (Goblin formula derivatives have worked), poisoned (specifically engineered compounds), and infected (engineered pathogens).
- **Sensory.** Visual acuity, low-light vision, auditory range, olfactory discrimination — all augmented. He can hear conversations across a room and read text at distances ordinary humans cannot resolve. The augmentation is also a **liability**: sensory overload episodes are recorded, particularly in crowd, subway, and combat-acoustic environments. Symbiote-period sensory amplification was catastrophic on first removal.

**Psychological impact of mutagenesis itself:** the mutation was experienced not as enhancement but as **a sudden severing from the body he had occupied for fifteen years**. The pre-bite Parker had a relationship with his physical limitations that, while miserable, was *his*; the post-bite Parker is an inhabitant of a body that does things without consulting him. The early issues' euphoria — the gleeful wall-crawling, the wrestling-ring debut — is, in retrospect, **hypomanic adjustment to acute somatic upheaval**, and it ends with Ben's death, after which the body becomes an instrument of penance rather than play. He never recovers the early delight in any sustained way. This is the medical-psychological hinge of his entire adult life: the gift became the tool, and the tool became the burden, within weeks.

---

## 3. INJURY LEDGER — CHRONOLOGICAL, NON-EXHAUSTIVE

The following is reconstructed from depicted trauma. The list is conservative; many lesser incidents are omitted for tractability. Each entry notes mechanism, probable acute medical sequelae, undocumented treatment, and where relevant, psychological impact.

**Year 1 (post-bite, late teens).**
- Multiple lacerations and contusions, wrestling debut and early street encounters. No medical contact; self-cleaned in the Forest Hills bathroom.
- **Ben Parker's death** — Peter is not physically injured. He sustains, in a single evening, what would become the index psychological trauma. **Somatic correlates:** appetite suppression for weeks (Aunt May references his not eating); insomnia; weight loss partially countering the post-bite anabolic gain.
- First serious combat injuries (Chameleon, Vulture, Doctor Octopus arcs). Concussion (Octopus, ASM #3) — depicted as unambiguous head trauma resulting in extended unconsciousness. No imaging, no observation period, no follow-up.

**Years 1–3 (Lee/Ditko core).**
- Repeated blunt trauma from Sandman, Electro (electrical burns and cardiac arrhythmia risk — survived without intervention; the mutation appears to confer some cardioprotection against electrical insult, though Electro has on multiple occasions induced loss of consciousness), Mysterio (toxin and hallucinogen exposure — undocumented neurochemical impact), Kraven the Hunter (toxin, blunt, blade).
- **The Master Planner sequence (ASM #31–33):** crushed under industrial machinery, depicted weight in tons; sustained pressing-out lift; subsequent underwater combat with significant blood loss; delivery of serum to dying Aunt May. Probable rhabdomyolysis; probable multiple stress fractures of long bones; probable internal hemorrhage. No hospitalization. He returned to school.
- **Lizard saliva and toxin exposures** (multiple): mild systemic chemical insult; brief delirium documented in at least one encounter.

**Years 3–7 (Lee/Romita through Conway).**
- **Captain Stacy's death (ASM #90):** falling masonry; Peter sustains contusions and a concussion but escapes the fatal injury Stacy absorbs. Psychological impact disproportionate to physical injury; the Ben-pattern is re-instantiated. *Bad day pattern* begins to be observable around the anniversary.
- **Death of Gwen Stacy (ASM #121):** Peter is uninjured in the immediate sense; the cervical-fracture mechanism is hers. Acute psychological collapse, fugue-like behavior for days, brief disordered combat with Green Goblin during which he is impaled by the Goblin's own glider mechanism through proximity rather than direct combat — **no, correction**: the impalement is the Goblin's, not Peter's. Peter sustains rage-driven combat injuries, multiple contusions, broken ribs (probable), and prolonged grief reaction. **He does not stop patrolling for more than a few days.**
- **First documented severe grief-state combat:** depicted as moving without spider-sense engagement, taking hits he would normally evade. This is observable across the record after every major loss — **a transient post-loss reduction in defensive efficacy** that suggests the spider-sense or his processing of it is mood-modulated.

**Years 7–15 (Wein/Wolfman/Stern).**
- Repeated fractures, dislocations, lacerations across a hundred combats. **Burglar's return arc (ASM #200):** confrontation with the man who killed Ben; physical injury moderate, psychological re-traumatization severe. Reports of intrusive memory in subsequent weeks.
- **Juggernaut sequence (ASM #229–230):** Peter is, by his own near-monologue, beaten beyond ordinary capacity for further exertion; he sustains repeated impacts that would kill a non-mutated human, including being driven through walls, masonry, and finally being held under by Juggernaut's mass. Probable: fractured ribs, fractured forearm, multiple Grade-III sprains, severe contusion, near-drowning. **No documented care.**
- **Hobgoblin combat injuries:** moderate; chemical exposures from Goblin formula derivatives produced, in one sequence, transient hallucinatory phenomena.

**Years 15–20 (Black Costume / Symbiote / Kraven / Marriage / 90s).**
- **Symbiote bonding (ASM #252 / Secret Wars context):** acute neuroendocrine entanglement with a foreign organism over weeks. Subjective symptoms during bonding: deepened sleep, vivid dreams, fatigue not relieved by rest, occasional micro-amnesia for early-morning hours during which the symbiote operated his body. **Separation:** acute sonic-induced detachment in the church bell tower sequence; sensory cascade, transient ataxia, exhaustion bordering on collapse, psychological aftermath of having been a passenger in his own body without knowing it. *Long-term sequelae:* persistent vulnerability to certain sonic and thermal stimuli; long-running unease about substances or arrangements that promise relief from exhaustion; **a permanent suspicion of his own desire for rest.** When he is offered ease, he refuses; when ease is forced on him, he panics. This is the medical-psychological lesion the symbiote left.
- **Kraven's Last Hunt (ASM #293–294, Web of Spider-Man #31–32, Spectacular #131–132):** shot with a high-caliber tranquilizer round at sufficient dose to drop him for nearly two weeks; **buried alive** in a casket under earth for that period; emerged by digging out unassisted. Acute sequelae: severe dehydration, electrolyte derangement, rhabdomyolysis from sustained immobility and the unburying exertion, hypoglycemia, vitamin and macronutrient deficit, decubitus pressure injury (likely), profound circadian disruption, and a degree of muscular atrophy that should have required weeks of rehabilitation. Psychological sequelae: a permanent **claustrophobic substrate** that he conceals well but that surfaces in enclosed-space sequences across subsequent decades; sleep disturbance involving suffocation-themed dreams; an aversion to being underground that he routes around when possible. **He resumed patrol within days.** No imaging, no labs, no psychological assessment. The Kraven event is, in clinical terms, the most under-treated severe trauma in his file, and the file is competitive.
- **Marriage period:** routine combat injury continues at baseline rate; the presence of a partner means some injuries are at least *seen* by another person — MJ becomes his de facto medical witness, and the historical record of his injuries during this period is therefore better, because she remembers them when he would prefer not to.
- **Spider-mutation incident** (the Six-Arms arc, ASM #100–102): self-induced transformation via experimental serum intended to remove powers; produced four additional arms for a period of days. Acute distress; rapid reversion via Morbius-blood–derived antidote. Psychological impact: a lasting **wariness of self-experimentation**, although he repeatedly breaches it under duress.
- **Clone Saga injuries** are largely identity-injuries rather than physical, but include: combat with multiple clones, exposure to genetic-instability sequelae (in cloned versions, not Peter himself, though he believed at one point he was the unstable one), and the prolonged psychological strain of ontological uncertainty.

**Years 20–35 (JMS through Civil War / OMD).**
- **Morlun encounters (Coming Home, The Other):** Morlun is one of the few opponents who can match or exceed his physical durability; the fights involve severe blunt trauma, extensive blood loss, multiple fractures. **In "The Other," Peter dies.** The death is metaphysically complicated and resolved via molting/rebirth, with mutations: organic web-shooters from spinneret-analog structures in the wrists; toxin-tipped stingers in the forearms (used reluctantly and rarely). Endocrine and glandular alterations of uncertain permanence; later writers regress the organic web-shooters with minimal medical explanation. **Psychological impact:** confrontation with a death he experienced rather than narrowly avoided; integration of the totemic mythology into his self-understanding (resisted, but partially absorbed); a renewed sense of the body as something that can be re-written without his consent.
- **Civil War period:** combat injuries from sustained Stark-side and then anti-Registration combat. **Unmasking** is not a physical injury but a catastrophic operational injury — the exposure of identity functions, in his nervous system, like the loss of a limb. He becomes hyper-vigilant, sleep-deprived beyond baseline, and operationally degraded for weeks.
- **Aunt May's shooting:** Peter is not the gunshot victim; the somatic toll is metabolic, sleep-related, and the resulting **"One More Day" arrangement** removes the marriage and rewrites the public-identity exposure. Whatever the metaphysical mechanism, his body emerges from that period in a state of unaccountable fatigue and a grief he cannot name because the conscious memory of what was lost has been edited. He is **bereaved without an object**, which is its own clinical category.

**Years 35–50 (Brand New Day, Big Time, Superior, Slott era).**
- Routine high-tempo combat injury continues. The **Superior Spider-Man period (ASM #698–700, Superior #1–31):** Otto Octavius performs a mind-swap; Peter inhabits Octavius's dying body and experiences death from within it; a fragment of Peter persists in his original body throughout Octavius's tenure as an observer. **Acute medical events during the Octavius tenure:** Octavius pursues a fitness, nutrition, and dental-hygiene regime Peter had neglected for decades — the body is, on Peter's return, in measurably *better* physical condition than he had ever maintained it (fillings replaced, musculature periodized, sleep regularized). The grim joke is that Peter's worst enemy took better care of his body than he did. **Psychological impact:** profound. He returns to a body that has been used without his consent — a re-instantiation of the symbiote violation at a more total scale — and to a life that has been re-arranged in his absence. He is also returned to a body that proves to him, by demonstration, that he could have lived less depleted. He largely fails to maintain the regime.
- **Parker Industries period:** for the first sustained period of adult life, Peter has resources for medical care. He does not, by any depicted evidence, use them. The collapse of the enterprise returns him to baseline precarity.

**Years 50–present (Spencer / Wells era).**
- Continued combat tempo; further confrontations with mortality (Kindred / Harry arc); intermittent severe injury without intervening recovery intervals adequate to a non-mutated body and arguably inadequate even to his.

---

## 4. SURGERIES, PROCEDURES, AND THE ABSENCE THEREOF

**Documented hospital admissions:** vanishingly few across the entire record. Several depicted ER visits as Peter Parker for civilian-presenting injuries; at least one extended hospitalization following civilian-mode trauma where the mutation could not plausibly account for rapid recovery without raising questions, and where May insisted.

**Surgeries:** none documented as Spider-Man (the cover would be impossible). As Peter Parker: minor sutures in episodic depictions; one wisdom-tooth extraction in the early ESU period that produced a brief depicted recovery sequence; dental restorations performed during the Octavius tenure (above).

**Self-treatment protocols:** extensive and ad hoc. The Forest Hills bathroom, and later the Chelsea / Tribeca / variously-located apartment bathrooms, function as his clinic. Standard kit: sutures (he can stitch his own non-dominant forearm; he learned in his late teens and improved), antiseptics, NSAIDs (used sparingly because they blunt the spider-sense in a way he dislikes), topical antibiotics, athletic tape, splinting materials. He sets his own dislocated fingers as a routine matter. He has reduced his own dislocated shoulder against a doorframe on multiple occasions. He **does not own a thermometer**, by inference from his behavior around illness, which is to ignore it.

**Imaging, lifetime:** essentially none post-bite. Any imaging would reveal the mutation. He has reasoned, plausibly, that he cannot afford the records to exist.

**Dental:** poor maintenance pre-Octavius, vastly improved post-Octavius restoration, slow regression thereafter.

**Optometry:** zero appointments post-bite. The myopia resolved; he has not needed correction in sixty years.

**Vaccination:** lapsed entirely post-bite; the mutation's pathogen resistance is broad but, as noted, not absolute.

---

## 5. SUBSTANCES

**Alcohol:** essentially abstemious. Documented to refuse offered drinks in social contexts, occasionally accept a single beer in extended-peer settings (Avengers downtime, wedding receptions, the rare bar scene with Logan or Johnny Storm) and nurse it. The metabolic acceleration almost certainly clears ethanol faster than baseline, rendering significant intoxication difficult; even allowing for this, the behavior reads as **principled hypercontrol** rooted in two convictions: that he cannot afford to be the one who fails a call, and — post-symbiote — that he cannot afford any reduction in volitional capacity.

**Tobacco:** never. No depicted use.

**Cannabis:** none depicted.

**Illicit substances:** none. He grew up in a household and an era that made the topic morally vivid; the canonical anti-drug arc (ASM #96–98) — in which his roommate Harry Osborn's pill addiction is the precipitating crisis — is formative. Peter's anti-drug stance is not theoretical; he watched a friend nearly die and a friend's father use that vulnerability against the friend. Lasting impact.

**Caffeine:** heavy, chronic, undisciplined. Multiple cups daily; convenience-store coffee; the coffee maker is, across decades of apartment depiction, the appliance kept cleanest. **


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS — SUBJECT: PARKER, P.B.

*A body's inventory. Compiled from longitudinal observational record, surveillance composite, and inferred granular detail consistent with sixty years of behavioral telemetry. Where the file says "observed," read: documented across multiple independent witness streams. Where it says "inferred," read: deduced from the constitutional and trauma load.*

---

## 1. STATURE, FRAME, AND THE BODY AT REST

Subject stands approximately five-foot-ten, weight cycling within a roughly fifteen-pound band that tracks financial stress (lower) and stable-residence intervals with M.W. (upper). Build is **deceptively lean** — what an examining physician would call "wiry mesomorphic," lat development and forearm flexor mass disproportionate to apparent overall musculature because his under-clothes silhouette is engineered, consciously or not, to read as ordinary. The mutation thickened cortical bone density and increased fast-twitch fiber recruitment without producing visible hypertrophy. He looks like a graduate student. This is operationally protective and he knows it.

**Resting posture, civilian frame.** Slight thoracic kyphosis when standing in line, on subways, at deli counters — a learned slouch, *not* anatomical, that subtracts about an inch and a half from his apparent height and rounds his shoulders into a posture his bullies in the early-1960s record would have recognized. The slouch is deepest in environments coded as J. Jonah Jameson–adjacent (newsroom, editorial), shallowest in laboratories and around children. **Seated:** he occupies less chair than his frame requires, knees drawn slightly together, ankles often hooked behind a chair leg — a containment posture. Hands tend to occupy themselves: a pen disassembled and reassembled, a paper napkin folded along orthogonal axes, a coffee-cup sleeve picked into a spiral.

**Resting posture, Spider-frame.** The slouch evaporates inside the suit. Mask on, the spinal column lengthens by an observable two to three inches; shoulder line drops and squares; weight settles onto the balls of the feet. Witnesses across the record consistently report the *crouch* — knees bent, hips low, one hand often touching the ground or surface, fingertips splayed. This is not theater; it is the proprioceptive default the mutation installs. He no longer has a comfortable way to stand straight. The crouch reads to civilians as "ready to spring." It reads to him as "neutral."

---

## 2. GAIT AND LOCOMOTION

**Civilian walk.** A loose, slightly bouncing stride, heel-strike marginally heavier on the left (old patellar injury, pre-bite, never reported). Average pace urban-quick — he was raised on Queens sidewalks and re-trained on Manhattan ones. He passes pedestrians on the outside, never the curb side. He waits at crosswalks even when the street is clear; this is identity discipline, performative ordinariness. **He never jaywalks in his civilian clothes.** The mutation makes him want to and the schema does not permit it.

**Stair behavior.** Two at a time, ascending, when alone or stressed. Single steps, deliberate, when accompanying others — particularly older companions; he slows to match May's cadence reflexively and the calibration persists with any senior-coded body around him. Descending, he tends to skip the last two steps regardless of context, a tell his enemies have never logged but which a longitudinal file would.

**Running, civilian-coded.** He throttles. The mutation could move him at roughly forty-plus miles per hour over short distances; in civilian dress he caps near a credible college-athlete sprint and adds visible labored breathing he does not actually require. The breath performance is one of his most consistent and least conscious deceptions.

**Movement under the mask.** Locomotion ceases to resemble walking in any conventional sense. Rooftop transit is a four-limbed lope at intervals, alternating with web-arc pendulums whose physics he has internalized at the level of cerebellar reflex; he chooses anchor points without conscious computation and his error rate on swing geometry is functionally zero except when emotionally compromised (Gwen-anniversary periods, post-loss days, the documented spike in misjudged swings during the Kraven aftermath). On vertical surfaces his weight distribution favors three points of contact at any moment; the fourth limb scouts. He inverts his head to the horizon — chin-toward-ceiling on walls, chin-toward-floor on ceilings — and his vestibular system has remapped accordingly so that "down" is operationally wherever his palms are.

**Landings.** He absorbs impact through ankle and knee flexion with the torso held remarkably still; this is a tell. Most enhanced operators absorb with the whole spine. He keeps the head level because the head is the camera and he wants the camera level.

---

## 3. HANDS

The most surveilled subsystem.

**Resting hand position, civilian.** Right thumb worries the pad of the right index finger in slow circles — an idle behavior that intensifies under cognitive load (test-taking, problem-solving, conversations he is performing his way through). Both hands carry **chemical-resistant calluses** along the medial pad of the palms and the inner phalanges — the signature of years of web-shooter cartridge-handling and homemade adhesive synthesis. The cuticles are bitten on the left hand, less so on the right; he is right-handed and the left bears more of the anxiety load.

**The web-shooter wrist mechanic.** Even out of costume, when startled, his middle and ring fingers twitch toward the proximal palmar surface of the wrist — the trigger position. This is a conditioned reflex roughly forty years deep at this point. He has been observed making the gesture while reaching for a falling coffee cup, while catching a dropped pen for a stranger, and once, on record, while shaking hands with a senator. He suppresses the gesture in front of the press almost successfully.

**Grip.** Calibrated to a granular fault. The most exhaustively documented somatic discipline in his entire repertoire is the **handshake**: the mutation gives him grip strength that can crush rebar, and the cognitive overhead of meeting a human hand without breaking it is, by his own occasional admission in interior monologue, never quite automatic. The handshake therefore registers as **slightly limp** — a soft, brief, withdrawing pressure that interlocutors often misread as timidity or insincerity. He cannot risk the alternative. The same calibration governs hugs (which he often initiates with the forearms and avoids with the chest), the holding of small objects (eggshells, contact lenses, the necks of children he picks up), and the opening of doors (he has installed a deliberate over-rotation of the wrist to compensate for the under-application of force, which produces a characteristic small twist that a careful observer would clock).

**Fingertips.** Setae-analog microstructures are not visible to the naked eye but produce a slight tackiness on contact with smooth surfaces — paper sticks to him momentarily; a glass tumbler released too fast will follow the fingers a centimeter before falling. He compensates by setting things down with a small lift-off motion. He pours liquids holding the vessel with extra fingers spread.

---

## 4. FACE — AT REST AND IN MOTION

**Resting face, unobserved.** Tired. The default expression when he believes no one is watching is a slight downward cast of the lateral brow with the lips relaxed and parted by perhaps a millimeter — a face that reads as quiet sadness or middle-distance exhaustion. Surveillance from across rooftops and through reflective surfaces captures this face more often than any other.

**Resting face, observed.** Flips within roughly four hundred milliseconds upon noticing observation, into a small, asymmetric smile favoring the right side, eyebrows lifting fractionally. This is the **civilian default mask**, and it is so consistent across decades that its absence in a given encounter is a high-confidence indicator that he is either unwell or angry.

**Eye behavior.** Brown, slightly close-set. Civilian: he makes initial eye contact, breaks within roughly two seconds, returns intermittently — the pattern of a chronically anxious-but-functional person, not a deceptive one. Under stress, the breaks lengthen and the returns become checking-glances rather than connection-glances. Under genuine threat in costume, the eye behavior is invisible behind the lenses, but the lenses themselves contract and expand on the mask — a mechanical articulation that, observers report, behaves with eerie congruence to actual eyelid musculature he is unconsciously firing underneath.

**Mouth.** Resting lips slightly chapped year-round (chronic mild dehydration). The lower lip is bitten on the inside, left-of-center; a small persistent ulcer there has been observed in successive close-quarters dental encounters. Smile asymmetric, right-dominant; the genuine Duchenne version, in which the orbicularis oculi engages and the outer eye corners crease, is **rare in the public record and frequent only in proximity to M.W., Aunt M., and the young hero peers he mentors**. The performed smile — for newscameras, J.J.J., strangers asking directions — disengages the eyes entirely.

**Micro-expressions under interrogation or moral conflict.** A characteristic upward flick of the inner brow that Ekman's coding would log as distress/sadness, suppressed within a half-second by the deflective smile. The flick is the truthful frame. The smile is the cover.

**Under the mask.** Speech patter increases by roughly forty percent in word-count-per-minute relative to civilian baseline; the mouth, freed from being observed, becomes more mobile, and the jokes — which the file has logged as a primary affect regulator — pour out at a rate inversely proportional to his perceived safety. He has been observed cracking jokes against opponents he knows can hear his pulse.

---

## 5. VOICE

Tenor, lightly nasal — Queens-coded with the consonants softened by university years and decades of code-switching. Speaking pace civilian: medium, with frequent self-interruption, sentence-restarts, and qualifier insertion ("I mean," "sort of," "I guess"). Pace in costume: faster, cleaner, fewer qualifiers — the role shed of his civilian apologetics.

**Laugh.** Two laughs in the record. The civilian one is a short exhaled "huh" with a closed-mouth grin, deployed at his own expense or as social lubricant. The genuine one — rare, almost always elicited by M.W. or by the absurdity of a particular villain's monologue — is a head-back, open-throated bark that surprises him. He often covers the mouth immediately afterward with a knuckle.

**Verbal tics.** "Oh, *boy*." "Yeah, no, that's — " "Look — " (sentence-opener when about to deliver bad news or refuse a request). The "Parker apology": an unsolicited acceptance of blame deployed roughly once per significant social encounter, often before any accusation has been made. Therapeutically diagnostic.

---

## 6. GROOMING AND SELF-PRESENTATION

Hair brown, thick, perpetually a week past needing a cut. Cut at home with scissors in poor periods; cut at the same Forest Hills barber when funds allow. Shampoo is whatever is on sale. He has worn the same three or four shirts in rotation across documented decades — soft cotton button-downs in blue, white, and a faded red, worn over white tees — replaced when destroyed, not when worn. Jeans single pair plus a backup. Shoes sneakers, replaced when soles fail; the laces are double-knotted on the right and single-knotted on the left (he has done this since middle school and cannot account for why).

**Shaving.** Inconsistent; he goes three to five days between, longer in low periods. The mutation accelerated facial hair growth marginally. He shaves with a safety razor over a sink, in three minutes, and nicks himself with implausible regularity given his reflexes — a tell that he is *not paying attention*, that his mind is elsewhere, that grooming is a low-priority background task he resents.

**Smell.** Soap, occasional drugstore deodorant, the faint chemical signature of web-fluid solvent that never quite washes off his cuffs, and — to anyone within close range — coffee. Under the mask after extended patrol: sweat-acid, fabric-musk, ozone from web discharge, and the metallic note of recent bleeding.

**Clothing under the suit.** Briefs, plain. Athletic socks. The suit is worn over bare skin elsewhere because layering compromises the adhesion math.

---

## 7. SLEEP ARCHITECTURE

Chronic short sleep, averaging across longitudinal record perhaps four-to-five hours per night, fragmented into a primary night block and a one-to-two-hour pre-dawn collapse after patrol. **Sleep onset latency** is low when he is exhausted, which is most of the time; long when grief is acute. **REM** appears intact but compressed; the file logs an unusually high frequency of vivid recall on waking, suggesting either REM rebound or chronic disruption.

**Sleep posture.** Defaults to fetal-on-the-right, knees drawn, dominant arm under the pillow. In shared beds, historically, he sleeps facing the partner with one hand on her hip or arm — proximity confirmation, anxious-attachment signature.

**The ceiling phenomenon.** Documented across multiple intimate witnesses and at least two ESU dormitory roommates: under acute stress or after intense patrol, the subject occasionally **sleeps adhered to the ceiling**, in a flattened prone configuration. He does not appear to do this consciously; he wakes up there, embarrassed, and detaches. The behavior correlates with PTSD-active periods and is a strong nocturnal stress index.

**Nightmares.** Recurrent. The recoverable content from witness reports clusters around (a) the warehouse and the burglar; (b) the bridge and the snap of a webline; (c) being unable to lift weight that is crushing someone he loves; (d) the symbiote period — moving without volition, watching his hands do things. He wakes from these silently — no scream, no jolt — sits upright, breathes for sixty to ninety seconds, and gets up. He does not return to sleep on a nightmare.

---

## 8. EATING

**Caloric load** enormous and inadequately met — the mutation requires perhaps six to eight thousand kilocalories on a moderate-activity day and substantially more on heavy combat days, against an income that has, for most of his life, supplied perhaps half of that. The somatic consequence is chronic mild ketogenic stress and the cognitive consequence is irritability spikes correlated with hour-of-day.

**Food behavior.** Eats fast. Eats standing. Eats on rooftops out of takeout containers. Pizza by the slice from the same handful of Queens and Manhattan storefronts whose owners do not ID him but who know to expect three or four slices folded longwise and consumed in under three minutes. Hot dogs from carts. Bodega sandwiches. Coffee, two-cream-two-sugar, in deli paper cups he reuses for refills until they leak.

**At the M. Parker table** he slows to deliberate, fork-and-knife civility, takes seconds without asking and thirds with a small apology, and has been observed eating wheatcakes he does not enjoy because she has made them and the alternative is unthinkable.

**With M.W.** he eats more, slower, and better; her presence is a documented re-regulator of his nutritional behavior.

**Hand-to-mouth tells.** When nervous he picks at food without consuming. When grieving he forgets to eat for stretches that show up as visible weight loss within forty-eight hours.

---

## 9. SEXUALITY AND INTIMACY

The file is, properly, sparse here, and the inferential framework respects that. What is observable:

**Touch hierarchy.** He is a person who initiates contact via low-stakes channels first — a hand on a shoulder, a brushed arm, a guiding palm on the back — and escalates only when the partner reciprocates. He does not touch without permission, including with long-established intimates; the consent-checking is so consistent it reads as somatic ethic.

**The strength-management problem.** Every documented intimate relationship has required him to develop a private calibration practice for the management of grip, weight, and reflex during physical proximity. Hugs are forearm-and-shoulder dominant. He sleeps on the side of the bed nearest the door, partly tactical, partly so that any startled-reflex motion in the night carries him away from the partner, not toward. He does not roughhouse. He has been observed flinching when a partner moves suddenly toward him — not from fear of attack, but from fear of his own reflex.

**Affective intimacy.** He is verbally and physically tender in established intimacy and somewhat tongue-tied at the threshold of new intimacy. He prefers his partner-of-record to initiate disclosure; he disclosure-reciprocates rather than disclosure-leads. With M.W. specifically, the somatic register shifts — the slouch softens into actual relaxation, the breath rate drops, and the smile reaches the eyes; this is the most regulated his nervous system has been documented to get outside of sleep.

**Post-intimacy behavior.** A characteristic stillness, a tendency to talk into the dark, occasional bouts of inappropriate humor as the parasympathetic system reasserts.

---

## 10. RITUALS, ROUTES, AND MICRO-PATTERNS

**Daily route signatures.** Subject habituates strongly. The Forest Hills–to-Manhattan path uses two preferred subway lines and one fallback; he stands rather than sits on trains and positions himself near a door but not in front of it. He scans the car on entry — a one-pass sweep, roughly two seconds — and a second sweep at each stop. He has been observed giving up his seat to elderly passengers within five seconds of their boarding, a reflex with no documented exception across the record.

**Coffee.** Same two or three vendors in any neighborhood he frequents; he develops parasocial rapport with the counter staff within three or four visits and remembers their names long past the point they remember his.

**Rooftop ritual.** Multiple witnesses and rooftop-camera composites describe a consistent **opening-of-patrol sequence**: he arrives at one of perhaps five preferred rooftops (a specific water tower in Chelsea recurs heavily across decades), perches on the edge for between forty seconds and four minutes, sometimes longer in winter, and *listens* — head tilted, breath slow. This is the closest behavior in the file to a contemplative practice. It is not religious in form but is functionally his prayer.

**Anniversary behavior.** Three dates produce reliable somatic and behavioral deviation: the night of the warehouse, the night on the bridge, and (variably reported) the date of N. Osborn's first reveal. On these dates he eats less, sleeps less, patrols longer, and routes patrol through specific cemeteries. He brings flowers he can afford. He does not speak during these visits and a long-lens camera will catch him with his mask half-off, just at the mouth.

**Refusal behaviors.** He declines alcohol with a small palm-up gesture and a joke about "early shift." He declines drugs with a flat "no thanks" and no joke. He declines money offered for services rendered in costume reliably and uncomfortably, often by webbing it back to the offerer mid-departure.

**Stress-coded micro-tells, ranked by reliability.**
1. The thumb-on-index circle (idle anxiety, near-constant low level).
2. The wrist-trigger twitch (startle).
3. The Parker apology (social discomfort).
4. The neck-roll, right-then-left, two cracks audible (transition into combat readiness, often performed in alleyways during mask-on).
5. The shallow exhale through pursed lips (recovery from acute stress, often after near-misses involving civilians).
6. A two-finger press to the bridge of the nose under the mask (cognitive overload; visible as a hand-to-face gesture from a distance).
7. Standing at full height, shoulders squared, slouch gone, in civilian clothes — **catastrophic anger**, exceedingly rare, and a high-priority signal in the file.

---

## 11. STATE-DEPENDENT SOMATIC SHIFTS — SUMMARY MATRIX

**Calm (rare; primarily in proximity to M.W. or in mentorship contexts with younger hero peers).** Slouch softens to genuine ease. Breath rate drops below baseline. Smile engages the eyes. Hands still. Humor warm rather than deflective. Eating slows. Eye contact lengthens and softens.

**Baseline civilian (default).** Slouch present, breath performance present, deflective smile available on demand, idle thumb-circle running, deflective humor at a steady clip, eye contact intermittent. Body subtly apologetic.

**Cognitive engagement (problem-solving, lab work, repair).** Posture forgets to slouch. Stillness deepens. Lips part slightly. Hands work continuously, often on multiple tasks in parallel. Verbal patter drops to near zero. Pulse slow. This is one of his most relaxed states and he does not know it.

**Acute social stress (newsroom, authority encounter, romantic disclosure threshold).** Slouch deepens. Verbal tics multiply. Thumb-circle accelerates. Eye contact fragments. The Parker apology fires. Skin flushes lightly across the cheekbones and the bridge of the nose.

**Threat onset (spider-sense triggers).** Posture re-organizes within roughly two hundred milliseconds: weight shifts to the balls of the feet, peripheral attention expands, the wrist-trigger position primes. In civilian dress, this is visible as a sudden *stillness* — he stops mid-motion, head turning fractionally toward the threat vector. A trained observer can locate the threat by following his eye-line during the freeze.

**Combat.** Locomotion becomes four-limbed and acrobatic; verbal output spikes into the joke-stream; expression behind the mask animates the lenses; pain response suppressed; injury registration delayed until disengagement. Heart rate runs well below what the metabolic demand would predict — the mutation has uncoupled exertion from cardiovascular stress to a remarkable degree.

**Post-combat decompression.** The shake — a fine tremor in the hands as catecholamines clear, often lasting two to ten minutes. He sits, usually on a rooftop edge, often eats something, often calls or thinks about calling someone he loves. The mask comes partly off — mouth and nose freed for air — but the top stays on. This is the most vulnerable somatic configuration in the file.

**Grief-acute (within hours of a loss).** Posture collapses. Eating ceases. Speech minimal. Eye contact zero. Movement either frozen (sitting in one position for hours) or compulsive (extended patrol with elevated risk acceptance). The face goes still — the smile-default disengages entirely and he forgets to put it back on. This is one of the only states in which strangers correctly read him as devastated.

**Intimacy (established).** The full somatic relaxation described under Calm, with additional softening of jaw and shoulder, slower blink rate, increased tolerance for sustained eye contact, lengthened conversational pauses without anxiety-fill, and — distinctive — the **return of the genuine laugh**.

**Mentorship of younger hero (e.g., M. Morales and analogues).** A specific h


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS

*Section 6 of the longitudinal dossier. Cross-referenced to Sections 1 (History), 3 (Psychological), and 4 (Psychiatric). All bonding behaviors below are derived from the published behavioral record and presented as the repeating template a total-surveillance file would have catalogued across six decades of observation.*

---

## 6.1 ORIGIN OF THE ATTACHMENT STYLE

The subject's attachment system is the product of three sequential structural events, each layered on the prior without displacing it. None of them have been clinically processed; they remain live.

**Stratum I — The pre-verbal loss (ages roughly 4–6).** Richard and Mary Parker die abroad on intelligence business; the child is delivered to the household of an aunt and uncle already in their late middle age. The earliest attachment figures vanish without ritual closure visible to the child, and the replacement figures are introduced under conditions of grief and apology. The behavioral residue of this stratum, observable decades later, is the subject's **chronic anticipatory mourning** — a baseline cognitive habit of pre-grieving the people in his life, rehearsing their loss before it occurs, as a covert insurance policy against being caught flat-footed again. This is visible in interior monologue across writers (the recurrent "what if this is the last time I see her" cadence around May), in his ritual goodbyes (he touches doorframes, looks back, lingers — micro-behaviors a watcher would tally), and in the way he writes letters and records messages he never sends.

**Stratum II — The originating moral wound (age ~15).** The Ben Parker murder is the structural event that converts an already-anxious attachment baseline into the **caregiving inversion**: he loves by guarding, and any harm to a loved one is metabolized as personal moral failure rather than external causation. The child who could not save the parent (Stratum I, retrospectively reframed) becomes the adolescent who *did not* save the uncle (Stratum II, immediately encoded). Attachment, from this moment forward, is no longer about being held — it is about holding. He cannot receive care without guilt, because to be cared for is to be the kind of person who failed Ben.

**Stratum III — Closeness as lethal vector (age ~20, Gwen Stacy).** The third stratum is the decisive distortion. Until Gwen, the schema permits the belief that *better protection* will resolve the danger — work harder, be more vigilant, never miss the warning. After the bridge, the schema mutates: **his very act of saving killed her.** The closer she was to him, the more lethal his proximity. This generates the operational rule that organizes every subsequent intimate relationship: *love is dangerous to the beloved; the optimum protective move is partial withdrawal.* He cannot fully act on the rule (his attachment hunger is too strong, his loneliness too acute), so he oscillates. The oscillation is the signature.

---

## 6.2 CLASSIFICATION

In the Ainsworth/Main framework, the subject would test as **anxious-preoccupied with strong disorganized intrusions under threat to the attachment figure.** In Bartholomew's four-category scheme, predominantly **preoccupied** with episodic **fearful-avoidant** flares. The disorganization is not generalized; it is *triggered specifically by perceived risk to the beloved*, at which point his behavior becomes contradictory and self-defeating in a textbook approach-avoidance pattern — he calls and hangs up, he shows up and then leaves, he reaches for the hand and pulls back.

The **caregiving system is hypertrophied** to the point of dominating the attachment system proper: he is more comfortable being needed than needing. Requests for help directed *at* him are processed instantly and prioritized over self-care; offers of help directed *to* him produce a characteristic deflection sequence — joke, redirect, change subject, leave room.

---

## 6.3 HOW HE BONDS — THE COURTSHIP AND CONSOLIDATION SIGNATURE

The bonding pattern is consistent enough across six decades and multiple intimates that a surveillance officer could checklist it.

**Phase 1 — Magnetism through deflective wit.** First contact is mediated by humor, almost without exception. The wit is a probe: it tests whether the other person can read affect under deflection. Those who laugh *and look past the joke* (MJ pre-eminently, also Felicia in her better moments, also several hero-peers) become candidates for actual attachment. Those who only laugh remain at the wit-perimeter — friendly, never intimate.

**Phase 2 — Acts of disproportionate service.** Within weeks of any relationship deepening, he begins performing small, asymmetric service acts that the recipient does not remember asking for: fixing the appliance, walking her home, showing up with food when she is sick, intervening with a landlord, repairing the bike. These are *love-gifts* but they are also **debt-creation in the opposite direction** — he prefers being the creditor of care because the debtor position activates his guilt circuit. A watcher tracking him would log a near-constant outflow of small unbilled labor.

**Phase 3 — Curated self-disclosure.** He discloses unevenly. Childhood material (Ben, May, the bullying, the science) comes out relatively easily, packaged in self-deprecation. Present-tense fears, financial precarity, exhaustion, the actual content of his nights, and — until forced — the secret identity itself, all come out late, partially, and usually under duress rather than initiative. The intimate is therefore in the strange position of feeling she knows him deeply (because he has been emotionally available and biographically forthcoming about the safe past) while in fact knowing very little about his current interior. This asymmetry is the seed of every major romantic rupture in his record.

**Phase 4 — The identity disclosure crisis.** Every long-form intimacy in his life eventually arrives at the unmasking event, and the manner of it is diagnostic. He has **never, in the published record, proactively and calmly disclosed the identity at a time of his choosing to a romantic partner.** MJ figured it out by observation (she had known for years before he knew she knew). Gwen never learned. Felicia learned by intuition and later by direct reveal under combat duress, and the relationship structurally could not survive his civilian self. May learned by his hospitalization. Harry learned through the Goblin lineage. The pattern: he allows the disclosure to be forced by circumstance rather than choose it, because choosing it would require him to credit the partner with the adult judgment to bear the knowledge — and crediting them that way would also be **handing them the danger.** Better, he reasons subconsciously, that they discover it and choose to stay than that he draft them into the danger by telling.

**Phase 5 — Consolidation behaviors.** Once consolidated, the bond is characterized by a specific texture: high warmth, high playfulness, high physical affection, *low logistical reliability*. He is late, he disappears mid-evening, he cancels plans, he is unreachable for hours at a stretch, he comes home bruised with implausible explanations. The partner is asked, implicitly, to accept a relationship structured around her own systematic deprioritization, with the compensation that when he is present he is *fully* present — warm, attentive, funny, tender. This is a real and not negligible compensation; it is also a structural form of intermittent reinforcement, the most behaviorally adhesive schedule there is. His intimates do not leave easily.

---

## 6.4 HOW HE DISTRUSTS

Distrust in this subject is **not paranoid** in structure. He does not generate suspicion ex nihilo; he generates it *retrospectively* when an attachment figure produces a behavior he cannot integrate, and his first move is to assume the failure is his.

His distrust signature:

- **Sudden affective withdrawal without confrontation.** Where a healthier subject might say "that hurt me, explain it," he goes quiet, finds a reason to leave, and processes alone. The partner experiences this as the door closing without knowing what she said.
- **Hypothesis-testing through proxy questions.** He will not ask "are you lying to me." He will ask three sideways questions about adjacent matters and triangulate. The cognitive style (convergent problem-solving, see §3) is brought to bear on the relationship as if it were a lab problem.
- **Toleration of low-grade betrayal with delayed reckoning.** He absorbs small betrayals (Harry's relapses, Felicia's relapses into theft, MJ's secrecies, even Stark's revealed bad faith in the Registration arc) for surprisingly long intervals, then ruptures suddenly when the accumulation crosses a threshold he did not announce.
- **Authority distrust as stable baseline.** With institutional figures — Jameson, the police, SHIELD, the Avengers' bureaucratic apparatus, government in general — distrust is *default* and trust must be earned. This is the inverse of his intimate posture, where trust is default and distrust must be earned, often past evidence that should have produced it sooner. The asymmetry is significant: he over-extends to the close and under-extends to the institutional, and both errors trace to the same source — the institutions failed Ben (the police did not catch the burglar; the system that should have protected his uncle didn't), while the intimates are loaded with the weight of what he could not give Ben.

---

## 6.5 HOW HE BETRAYS

He does not betray in the ordinary register — no infidelity of consequence in the canonical record, no betrayal of confidence for gain, no instrumental use of intimates. The betrayals he *does* commit are of a specific and consistent kind:

**Betrayal by omission.** He withholds information the partner needs in order to make informed choices about her own life — the danger she is in by association, the state of his health, the depth of his financial precarity, the identity of the friend who just died. The withholding is always framed (internally) as protection. The partner consistently experiences it as condescension and as a refusal to be partnered with as an adult.

**Betrayal by unilateral decision-making in crisis.** Under acute threat to a loved one, his executive function narrows to single-objective protection and he makes choices *for* the protected party that they would not have authorized — the most extreme case being the Mephisto bargain, but the same pattern recurs in smaller forms: hiding her in a safe house without consultation, breaking off the engagement "for her safety," disappearing for weeks on a case without communication. The pattern reads, to the partner, as her **agency being treated as a luxury his guilt cannot afford.**

**Betrayal by chronic unavailability.** The slow betrayal of consistently choosing the patrol over the relationship at the margin. Each individual instance is defensible; the cumulative pattern is not.

He has, notably, **almost never betrayed by malice, vanity, or gain.** This is a load-bearing fact about him. The betrayals are all generated by the protective schema running over the autonomy of the protected.

---

## 6.6 HOW HE REPAIRS

Repair is the operation in which his attachment system is most visibly competent and most visibly limited.

**Competent:** He apologizes readily and without ego defense. He does not relitigate. He accepts that he was wrong even when he was partly right, often over-accepting. He performs reparative service (returns to Phase 2 behaviors with redoubled intensity). He shows up. He remembers anniversaries, small preferences, the names of the partner's siblings and coworkers — his memory for the granular life of the beloved is photographic and warm.

**Limited:** He cannot perform the deeper structural repair that would require **changing the conditions that produced the rupture.** He will apologize for missing the dinner; he will not stop missing dinners. He will apologize for not telling her about the injury; he will not start telling her about injuries. The repair is *affective*, not *structural*, because structural repair would require him to reduce the protective hyperfunction, and the protective hyperfunction is non-negotiable to him — it is the schema, and the schema is the wall against the Ben-grief.

So the repair cycle is: rupture, withdrawal, return with warmth and apology, brief honeymoon, slow drift back to baseline, same rupture. Across years, this exhausts even the most patient intimate.
