The MJ relationship has endured this cycle more times than any other in the record, surviving because (a) MJ has unusually robust autonomy and her own life, (b) she has metabolized the schema and *expects* it, which is itself a sad accommodation, and (c) the warmth in the present-tense moments is genuinely large.

---

## 6.7 INTIMACY AND DEPENDENCY

**Sexual intimacy** is, in the record, depicted as warm, mutual, and uncomplicated by ordinary dysfunctions, but is **conditioned on emotional safety in a way that makes it episodic rather than continuous.** Periods of high external threat are correlated with reduced intimacy initiation by him (he displaces the somatic energy into patrol and into his own self-soothing — sleep deficit, food, work).

**Emotional intimacy** is asymmetric in his preferred mode: he prefers to be the receiver of disclosure and the giver of reassurance, not the reverse. Asked direct questions about his interior, he deflects to humor or to inquiry about her. The partner who insists on parity ("no, I asked how *you* were doing") gets, after sufficient pressure, a partial honest answer delivered with visible discomfort. He can do it. He does not initiate it.

**Dependency on him** is something he tolerates and quietly encourages — he is more comfortable when the loved one needs him for something concrete. **Dependency by him** is the harder direction. He will not ask for money, will not ask for help with a task he can plausibly do himself, will not ask to be cared for when ill (May has historically had to pin him down), will not ask for emotional support after a loss (he isolates, then re-emerges).

The result is a relationship topology in which he is **the giver-of-care and the withholder-of-need.** This produces, in the partner, over time, a specific kind of loneliness — being with someone who is fully present and yet structurally inaccessible at the deepest layer. The partners who have stayed have learned to read the deep layer through indirect signs: which jokes he is making, how late he came in, whether he ate, the small set of physical tells (the favoring of a rib, the staring out the window at nothing) by which his interior is legible to those who have decoded him. **He is read more than he is told.**

---

## 6.8 THE RELATIONAL TEMPLATE, ITERATED ACROSS ALL CATEGORIES

The same template recurs across every relationship class. The cast changes; the structure does not.

**With maternal figures (May, and by extension every older woman in his orbit — Anna Watson, Madame Web in the mentor variant).** Hyper-protective; will sacrifice anything; will not burden them with his fear. Conceals injury, financial trouble, romantic distress. Calls regularly, with a specific cadence — short, cheerful, asks about her, reassures her of his wellbeing whether or not he is well. The May relationship is the prototype and the cathexis-center; every other older woman in his life receives a fractional version of the same pattern.

**With paternal/mentor figures (Ben in memory, Captain Stacy, Curt Connors, Reed Richards, Stark, the various Avengers elders).** Eager to please; absorbs their values quickly; experiences their disappointment as catastrophic and their approval as warming but never quite sufficient. **Each one is, structurally, a candidate Ben-surrogate**, and each one's failure or death re-wounds the original schema. The Stark arc is the most legible case: he extends the trust of a son, follows him into a position he should have refused, and when Stark's project reveals its costs, the rupture is not just political — it is a re-experience of paternal failure, with the corresponding regression into the lone, untrusting posture. After Stark, he has been considerably more wary of paternal authority.

**With romantic partners (Betty Brant, Liz Allan, Gwen, MJ, Felicia, Carlie, the cycle).** Full template as detailed in §6.3–§6.6. The longest-standing variant — MJ — is the only one in which the template has been (intermittently) interrupted by a partner whose own resources and insight are sufficient to force structural conversation. Even there, the interruptions are episodic.

**With peers (Harry, Flash in his redemption arc, Johnny Storm, the rotating Avengers cohort).** Loyalty disproportionate to the peer's actual conduct. Forgives serially. **Harry is the apotheosis** — Peter forgives Harry for offenses (drug relapses, betrayals, attempts on his life under the Goblin influence) that would terminate most friendships, because the friendship is loaded with the residue of the formative years and with Peter's structural inability to abandon someone he reads as struggling. Flash Thompson's late-life heroism (Agent Venom) and Peter's warmth toward him in those years are a quiet demonstration of the same trait: prior wrongs are filed under "we were young," and the present-tense person is given a clean slate, possibly cleaner than they have earned.

**With protégés (Miles Morales, Anya Corazon, Gwen Stacy of the Spider-Family, Silk, others).** Here the template inverts and the subject is in the Ben-position. The behavior here is among his healthiest in the record: warm, patient, technically generous (he hands over the work, lets them have the win, corrects gently), and explicit about the lessons he was taught. This is **reparative caregiving** in the Eriksonian generativity sense, and it is the area of his relational life in which he is least conflicted. A watcher would note that he is freer, lighter, more verbally available, and more willing to *receive* affection from the younger heroes than from any other category — because the asymmetry runs in the direction his schema authorizes, and the protective debt is being paid forward in a form that does not require him to be vulnerable in return.

**With antagonists.** Even here the template asserts itself. He pities those whose damage he can read (Octavius, Connors, Marko, Toomes in his more rounded depictions, even Osborn at the level of Norman-the-broken-father underneath the Goblin). He attempts repair where repair is possible. He extends trust prematurely. He is wounded when the trust is broken. He repeats. The **enemy-as-damaged-person** schema is a direct extension of the caregiving inversion, applied beyond its prudent range.

**With institutions.** Inverted distrust as noted in §6.4 — he begins from suspicion and requires earning. Even institutions he has served (the Avengers, the Future Foundation, the Fantastic Four during his tenure) he holds at a particular distance; he will work alongside them, he will not be of them, and he reserves the right to walk away on a moral disagreement. This too is templatic: institutions did not protect Ben, so institutions cannot be trusted to protect what he loves.

---

## 6.9 THE MASTER PATTERN

Reduced to its skeleton, the template is:

> **Approach with warmth and wit. Establish service-asymmetry in his favor. Disclose the past freely, the present sparingly. Conceal the danger and the cost. Be fully present when present, structurally unavailable at the margin. Absorb small betrayals; rupture suddenly on accumulation; withdraw without confrontation; return with apology and reparative service; do not change the structural conditions; repeat. Protect by deciding for the other; experience their objection to that protection as a wound rather than as information. Receive care reluctantly; give care reflexively. Read the other deeply; allow oneself to be read only through indirection. Forgive serially; expect to be left and pre-grieve accordingly; be surprised when stayed with; be unable to fully trust the staying.**

This is the relational fingerprint. It appears, with category-appropriate variation, in every documented relationship across six decades, and it is generated, recursively and without remission, by a single unprocessed grief and the moral framework he built on top of it to keep functioning. The framework works — he functions, he loves, he is loved — and it costs him, and the people who love him, exactly what such frameworks cost. A surveillance officer with sixty years of tape would conclude, correctly, that this is a man who has never stopped trying to save his uncle, and that everyone he has ever loved has, in some hour of the night, been a stand-in for the man on the floor of that house in Forest Hills.


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# SECTION 6 — DEFENSES & COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS

*The full architecture of the subject's psychological self-protection, ranked by primitiveness in the Vaillant tradition (mature → neurotic → immature → psychotic), with behavioral operationalization, ignition conditions, observable tells, and longitudinal failure modes. Compensatory structures — those secondary scaffoldings the subject has built around the defenses to make a workable life — are catalogued in parallel, separated into adaptive (load-bearing, prosocial) and maladaptive (cost-shifting, self-destructive). This is the operating system; what runs on top of it is the behavior catalogued elsewhere in this file.*

---

## 6.1 OVERVIEW — THE SHAPE OF THE ARCHITECTURE

The subject's defensive structure is unusually **top-heavy in the mature register**, with a robust neurotic floor, episodic immature breakthroughs only under extreme load, and effectively zero psychotic-level defenses in the operative record. This is, structurally, the defense profile of a high-functioning, conscientious, traumatized adult — not of a personality-disordered subject. The architecture has held for six decades of catastrophic stress, which is itself the most important data point: the system does not collapse. It bends, it leaks, it costs the subject enormously to maintain — but it does not fragment.

The defining feature of his architecture, distinguishing it from a textbook "healthy mature defenses" profile, is that **the mature defenses are themselves in the service of an underlying pathological schema**. His humor, sublimation, altruism, and intellectualization are not deployed to *resolve* the core wound (the responsibility schema rooted in Ben Parker's death). They are deployed to make the wound *operable* — to permit continued function around an unmetabolized injury. The defenses are how he carries the shrapnel, not how he removes it. This is critical: a clinician encountering only the mature register would underdiagnose; only the longitudinal record makes the cost visible.

Defenses are ranked below from most to least mature, with operational detail.

---

## 6.2 MATURE DEFENSES (Vaillant Level IV)

### 6.2.1 Humor — the first line, the loudest tell

The single most operationally dominant defense in the record. Behavioral signature: **verbal patter, pun structure, mock-formality, self-deprecation, and absurdist redirection**, deployed in real time during physical combat, social discomfort, grief, and physical pain. The patter has identifiable subtypes:

- *Combat patter* — short jokes timed to punches, escalating in density as the fight worsens. The patter is genuinely tactical (it destabilizes opponents, slows their tempo, projects confidence he does not feel) but its **primary function is intrapsychic**: it modulates his own affect by forcing exhalation, lowering autonomic arousal, and creating a meta-position from which the pain is happening to a character he is narrating rather than to him directly. Surveillance value: the **density-per-minute of the patter correlates inversely with felt safety**. He is loudest when most afraid. Silence in combat is the meaningful signal — silence means either tactical concentration on a peer-level threat or grief breakthrough.
- *Social patter* — self-deprecating one-liners deployed to defuse civilian social awkwardness, deflect compliments, and prevent intimacy escalation past thresholds he is not ready for. The recurring "loser-genius" persona (showing up late, schlumpy, with an excuse) is partially this defense reified into a persistent mask.
- *Grief-adjacent humor* — the darkest register, often deployed alone or in interior monologue, recognizable by its **clipped rhythm and bitter terminal beat**. Surveillance value: this is the variant a careful observer can read as a depressive marker.

Failure mode: in extreme grief states (immediately post-Gwen, immediately post-May-shooting, deep Kraven-aftermath) the humor *cuts out entirely*, replaced by either silence or terse functional speech. The absence is diagnostic.

### 6.2.2 Sublimation — the role itself

The entire Spider-Man enterprise is, in defensive terms, a structural sublimation of grief, guilt, rage, and unmetabolized aggression into prosocial channels. Every mugger thrown into a dumpster is, at the somatic level, a swing he did not take at the burglar in 1962. The defense is exceptionally effective because the sublimated output is genuinely valuable — third parties benefit, the subject reduces his own internal pressure, and the moral framework permits him to interpret the relief as virtue rather than catharsis.

The risk is *sublimation insufficiency under load*: when the volume of internal pressure exceeds what the role can absorb, the residue manifests as somatic neglect, sleep collapse, or romantic sabotage. The defense channels the aggression but does not channel the grief well — grief leaks into the somatic and attachment systems regardless.

### 6.2.3 Altruism — chronic, occasionally pathological

True altruism in the Vaillant sense: he derives genuine satisfaction from others' wellbeing, and that satisfaction is one of the few reliable mood stabilizers he has. Distinguishable from reaction formation because the warmth precedes any threat and is present in contexts where no defensive function is being served (mentorship behavior with younger heroes; quiet small kindnesses to neighbors and students).

Pathological tipping point: when altruism becomes **non-discretionary** — when he cannot refuse a call for help even at catastrophic personal cost, even when better-positioned responders exist, even when his refusal would be morally correct. The defense crosses into compulsion. This is the lever every sophisticated antagonist (Norman Osborn most surgically) has learned to pull.

### 6.2.4 Anticipation — partial and selective

He anticipates threats with great skill in tactical and engineering domains (web-shooter refills, costume redundancy, evacuation planning during fights). He anticipates **emotional** threats poorly — he does not plan for grief, does not prepare for anniversaries, does not pre-position social supports before known-difficult dates. The defense is highly developed in the instrumental register and atrophied in the affective register, which is itself a tell about which feelings he permits himself to know in advance.

### 6.2.5 Suppression — operational, with cost

Capable of consciously deferring affect until task completion. He can put grief in a box, fight a city-block fight, and open the box later. The cost is that the box rarely gets opened on schedule, and the contents compound. Suppression is being used in the place where **processing** should occur. Over decades, this produces the stacked, unmetabolized grief load documented elsewhere in this file.

---

## 6.3 NEUROTIC DEFENSES (Vaillant Level III)

### 6.3.1 Intellectualization — pre-traumatic and load-bearing

The earliest documented defense in the record, predating the bite. Under emotional pressure he migrates into chemistry, engineering, taxonomic problem-decomposition. The web-shooters themselves are a grief-coping artifact as much as a tool: he designed them in a weekend that immediately followed his transformation, in the same period he was processing a radical change in his somatic identity. The pattern recurs — major emotional shocks are followed within days by **technical projects of disproportionate ambition** (costume redesigns, web-fluid reformulations, tracer upgrades, the Parker Industries gambit in the wake of identity disruption).

Surveillance value: **a sudden flurry of lab work is an affective signal, not a research signal.** Track the projects, infer the underlying loss.

### 6.3.2 Reaction Formation — toward Jameson and pity-objects

Most visible in the Jameson relationship: a man who has publicly defamed him for decades, whom he saves repeatedly, whose paper he funds with his own photo sales. The conscious framing is duty and pragmatism; the structural form is reaction formation against the rage that would be appropriate. Similar pattern toward antagonists he pities (Octavius, Connors, Marko, even Osborn in some configurations) — the warmth and protective concern toward people who have repeatedly tried to kill him or his loved ones exceeds what a pure ethical framework requires and reads as defense against the murderous rage he refuses to countenance in himself.

### 6.3.3 Undoing — the engine of the compulsion

Every life saved is, structurally, an attempt to undo Ben's death. This is the most important neurotic defense in the architecture because it explains the **compulsive quality** of the heroism that altruism alone would not predict. A purely altruistic agent could rest after sufficient good done. An undoing agent cannot, because the original act cannot be undone. The defense generates an infinite debt with an infinite repayment schedule. It is also why retirement attempts fail — retirement is not an option when the debt is ontological.

### 6.3.4 Displacement — partial, mostly toward objects

Rage that cannot be discharged at appropriate targets (Ben's killer, dead; Norman Osborn, periodically dead; the abstract structural conditions that produce villains) is displaced onto property — walls punched, web-shooters thrown, lab equipment broken in private. Rarely displaced onto persons. The selectivity of the displacement (objects yes, people no) is itself a marker of the strength of his conscience-structure.

### 6.3.5 Isolation of Affect — episodic, post-trauma

After major losses, a window of clipped, procedural functioning in which the affective tone is detached from the content. Kraven-aftermath issues, post-Gwen issues, post-symbiote-removal issues all show this pattern: he describes catastrophic events in flat declarative sentences, conducts post-mortems with the affect of a lab report. The isolation breaks down later, usually in private and usually somatically (insomnia, appetite loss, the pacing).

### 6.3.6 Rationalization — selective and self-punishing

Notably, his rationalization runs **against his own interest** — he rationalizes others' behavior charitably (Jameson is just stressed; MJ deserves better; Harry can be saved) and rationalizes his own failures harshly (he should have been faster, smarter, present). This is rationalization in the service of the responsibility schema rather than against it. A textbook rationalizer would protect the self; this subject uses the defense to indict the self.

### 6.3.7 Repression — selective and leaky

He does not appear to repress traumatic content in the classical sense (the memories are accessible and intrusive). He does repress **legitimate self-interest** — the desires to rest, to be cared for, to receive without immediate reciprocation, to be angry at people who deserve it. These return as somatic symptoms, sabotage of intimacy, and the periodic exhaustion crashes.

---

## 6.4 IMMATURE DEFENSES (Vaillant Level II) — RARE BUT PRESENT

### 6.4.1 Acting Out — short bursts, followed by remorse

Documented in narrow windows: post-Gwen rage at Osborn, post-May-shooting confrontation with the Kingpin, occasional unrestrained combat overruns when grief is acute. These are time-limited (minutes to hours, rarely days) and reliably followed by **excessive self-punishment** that returns the system to its baseline over-controlled state. The acting-out is therefore self-correcting; it does not establish itself as a stable pattern.

### 6.4.2 Passive Aggression — minor, intimate-context only

Restricted almost entirely to romantic relationships under stress: late arrivals, vague explanations, deflective humor used to avoid difficult conversations, broken plans framed as accidents that are partially chosen. Not a primary defense; rarely deployed outside intimacy.

### 6.4.3 Somatization — extensive but unrecognized as defense

He converts unmetabolized affect into physical complaint with great reliability — back pain, exhaustion, frequent minor illnesses (especially in the Lee-era and JMS-era runs). The body carries the affect the cognition will not. Because his framework conceives the body as instrument, the somatic load is read as wear-and-tear rather than as signal. This is one of the architecture's most significant blind spots.

### 6.4.4 Hypochondriacal *inversion* — anti-hypochondria

The mirror of the standard immature defense: he systematically *under-reports* physical symptoms, dismisses injuries, declines medical attention. The function is identical to hypochondria (avoidance of an underlying issue) but the surface presentation is opposite. The underlying issue avoided is **the legitimacy of his own needs**.

### 6.4.5 Fantasy — minimal

Striking by its near-absence. He does not retreat into compensatory fantasy; his interior life is bracingly realistic and often grimmer than his external situation warrants. The one borderline-fantasy register is the **alternative-life imagining** ("what if I'd never been bitten," "what if I quit") which appears in interior monologue at low points but is reliably terminated by a return to duty rather than indulged.

---

## 6.5 PSYCHOTIC-LEVEL DEFENSES (Vaillant Level I) — ABSENT

No documented delusional projection, denial of external reality, or distortion in the operative record. Reality-testing is intact even under extreme load (Kraven entrapment, Superior dispossession, symbiote bonding) — he correctly identifies what is happening to him in each case, even when he cannot act on it. The architecture has no psychotic floor; under-load, the system regresses only to the immature register and then recovers.

---

## 6.6 POSITIVE COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS (Adaptive Scaffolding)

These are not defenses proper but the secondary structures built around the defenses that make a workable life possible.

- **The mentorship vector.** Acting as a Ben-figure to younger heroes (Miles Morales, the broader Spider-Family configurations, occasional civilians) is reparative — it lets him *occupy* the position whose loss he could not prevent, and produces genuine therapeutic benefit. The mentorship is one of the very few contexts in which he permits himself to receive admiration without immediate deflection.
- **The science identity.** The lab persona is a refuge in which his competence is uncomplicated by moral debt. He can be good at chemistry without owing anything to anyone, which is a state otherwise unavailable to him.
- **The chosen-family network.** May, MJ (across configurations), Aunt Anna in some periods, a small set of hero-peers — a deliberately small, intensely curated group within which the deflective mask drops in graduated stages. He has invested in the *quality* of attachment to compensate for the *anxiety* of attachment.
- **The moral framework itself.** While the framework is the source of his pathology, it is also the source of his coherence. It tells him what to do every morning. It prevents the catastrophic moral drift that comparably powered, comparably traumatized agents undergo. The framework is a load-bearing compensation for the chronic dysthymic substrate.
- **The patter as social lubricant.** Even when the humor is defensive, it produces real social goods — it makes him welcome in rooms, it gives bystanders permission to relax during crises, it humanizes a being who could otherwise be terrifying.
- **Reading and continued learning.** Documented across decades: he reads voraciously, including outside his technical fields. This is genuine integration, not just intellectualization — he uses the reading to update his worldview, not only to escape from it.
- **Photography.** The camera-eye discipline is compensatory in two registers: it provides income, and it provides an aesthetic-observational stance that converts ugly events into composed images, a controlled form of witnessing.

---

## 6.7 NEGATIVE COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS (Maladaptive Scaffolding)

- **Compulsive workaholism.** Patrol layered atop work layered atop (formerly) school. The compensation is for the intolerable sensation of *not being useful in this moment*. The cost is sleep, health, relationships, and the periodic burnout collapses.
- **Somatic self-neglect.** Skipped meals, skipped sleep, untreated injuries, no medical follow-up after catastrophic events. The body is treated as an instrument owed to others; the neglect is the price he charges himself for occupying it.
- **Financial under-functioning.** A man of his cognitive capacity should not be chronically broke. The under-functioning is behaviorally meaningful — it expresses the belief that he does not deserve material stability, and it provides a *visible* form of suffering that satisfies the punitive substrate without him having to acknowledge what is happening.
- **Threshold-sabotage of intimacy.** As intimacy approaches the point at which loss would be unbearable, behaviors emerge that create distance (vagueness about whereabouts, cancellation, the deflective humor stiffening into a wall, in extreme cases the unilateral termination). The pattern protects against the *anticipated* grief at cost of the *actual* relationship.
- **The cheerful-loser persona.** A curated mask presented to most contacts (Jameson, casual acquaintances, neighbors, civilian coworkers). It pre-emptively lowers expectations so that disappointment cannot wound. The cost is that it makes legitimate professional and social ascent nearly impossible — he is too convincing in the role.
- **Inability to say no.** Documented and weaponized. Any request framed as protective duty bypasses his veto. The compensation is for the original "no" that resulted in Ben's death; the cost is exploitability and exhaustion.
- **Caffeine over-reliance.** Substitute for the rest he will not permit himself.
- **Apology inflation.** He apologizes routinely, including for things that are not his fault and including to people whose own behavior warrants apology to him. The compensation is for the original unutterable apology he owes a dead man; the cost is a permanent posture of moral debt that others learn to exploit.
- **Avoidance of clinical contact.** No therapy, no medical workups, no sustained engagement with helping professionals. The compensation is for the loss of volitional control he experienced under the symbiote and under Octavius; the cost is the absence of any external interruption to the loop.

---

## 6.8 IGNITION CONDITIONS — WHICH DEFENSE FIRES WHEN

A surveillance-grade mapping of triggers to responses, derived from the longitudinal record:

- *Acute physical threat to self only.* Humor (combat patter) + anticipation (tactical) + suppression (affect deferred). Stable.
- *Acute physical threat to a third party.* Sublimation + altruism dominant; humor present but thinned; suppression near-total.
- *Acute physical threat to an attached figure.* Suppression collapses; brief acting-out window possible; afterward, isolation of affect for hours to days; then somatization; then a flurry of intellectualization (project work).
- *Loss of an attached figure.* Initial isolation of affect (hours to days); brief acting-out possible; transition to chronic undoing-driven hyperactivity in the role; somatic neglect intensifies; intimacy sabotage with surviving figures; long-tail dysthymic deepening.
- *Defamation, injustice toward self.* Reaction formation (toward the defamer); rationalization (against the self); humor (with bitter beat); suppression of legitimate anger.
- *Romantic intimacy approaching threshold.* Threshold-sabotage; humor stiffening to wall; vague absences; the cheerful-loser persona reinforced.
- *Loss of volitional control (symbiote-class threat).* No defense available; the architecture is built around the assumption of agency. He fragments into observer mode, then mobilizes maximum intellectualization to retake the body. Post-event: extensive avoidance behavior (substance abstemiousness, no therapy, no further alien contact).
- *Moral compromise demand (e.g., killing request, registration pressure).* Held-line; intellectualization deployed to articulate the line; if the line is breached under coercion, catastrophic guilt response and corrective over-reaction (the Civil War arc as the case-study).
- *Success and material stability.* Paradoxically destabilizing — triggers sabotage behavior, financial under-functioning re-emerging, threshold-sabotage of accompanying intimacy. He cannot inhabit stability because stability is incompatible with the debt.

---

## 6.9 LONGITUDINAL FAILURE MODES

The architecture has three documented failure modes, none of which produce psychotic collapse but all of which produce significant operational and personal damage:

1. **Burnout collapse.** When suppression has compounded past the system's capacity, the subject enters a window (days to weeks) of reduced functioning — slept-through patrols, missed work, intimacy ruptures, fights badly lost. Recovery is typically catalyzed by a crisis that re-activates the responsibility schema; he does not recover by *resting* but by being *summoned*. This is a maladaptive recovery pattern that perpetuates the cycle.
2. **Abdication attempt.** Periodically (Clone Saga civilian-life attempt, post-OMD configurations, retirement musings throughout) he tries to walk away. The attempts fail because the undoing defense cannot tolerate a state in which the role is not being performed; civilian life feels like *omission*, and omission is the original sin. He returns to the role, usually within issues, and the return is framed as choice but is structurally compulsion.
3. **Catastrophic moral concession.** Under sufficient pressure on an attached figure (the OMD trade being the clearest case), the architecture will sacrifice its own coherence — including marriage, including continuity of self-narrative — to preserve the attached figure. The defenses fail upward, into a frame in which the unbearable loss is averted at any cost to the system itself. The post-concession period is characterized by diffuse low-grade depression and a slightly more brittle defensive profile that takes years to re-stabilize.

---

## 6.10 SUMMARY — WHAT THE ARCHITECTURE IS FOR

The defensive structure is, in aggregate, an extraordinarily elegant solution to an unsolvable problem: how to remain a functional, prosocial, attached agent while carrying an unmetabolized originating trauma, a punishing moral schema, and a job that re-traumatizes its holder by design. The mature defenses do most of the visible work; the neurotic defenses do most of the load-bearing; the immature defenses provide a narrow pressure-release valve; the psychotic floor is empty.

The system's signature property is that **it works at the cost of the person operating it**. He is, in defensive terms, a building whose support beams are made of his own body. The architecture's longevity is a tribute to his intelligence, conscience, and stubbornness. It is also the reason he is, by any reasonable clinical standard, in chronic and unaddressed need of care.

The single intervention that would most transform the architecture is the one he will most reliably refuse: permission, granted by himself to himself, to be the *recipient* of the protective concern he extends to everyone else. Every defense in the stack is configured to prevent that permission from being granted. Until it is, the system will continue to run — beautifully, prosocially, and at full cost — exactly as it has for six decades.


## Longitudinal Psychological Profile

# LONGITUDINAL PSYCHOLOGICAL PROFILE — SUBJECT: PARKER, PETER B.

*Decade-by-decade clinical formulation. Frameworks invoked: Vaillant's defense hierarchy; Beck's cognitive-distortion taxonomy; Bowlby/Main attachment models; Linehan's affect-regulation schema; Young's schema therapy; Janoff-Bulman on shattered assumptions; Herman on complex trauma; Erikson on lifespan tasks. All inferences indexed to behavioral evidence in the published record.*

---

## I. PRE-BITE BASELINE (childhood through age ~15; AF #15, Untold Tales, ASM #-1, retrospective issues)

**Affect regulation.** Constricted at baseline. The boy depicted at the Parker breakfast table is affectively muted in a way that reads as adaptive numbing to the early parental loss — affect is present (curiosity, hurt at peer rejection) but expression is throttled, channeled into Aunt May's emotional comfort rather than self-disclosure. The dominant regulatory strategy is **cognitive absorption**: he removes himself from affectively charged environments (the cafeteria, the dance) into texts and microscopes. There is no observable rage repertoire; anger at Flash Thompson is swallowed and recoded as resigned shame. The somatic correlate — flinch posture, narrow shoulders, the lowered chin in Ditko's renderings — is the body of a child who has learned that visibility costs.

**Cognitive style.** Already crystallized as **fluid, convergent, analogical, systems-oriented**. He thinks in mechanisms. The decision in the originating week to design web fluid and shooters from scratch — chemistry, materials engineering, micro-mechanical fabrication — over a span of days is not merely a feat; it is a *coping artifact*. Problems with closed analytic solutions are where his nervous system rests. Cognitive vulnerabilities present from the outset: a **personalization bias** (he reads peer rejection as evidence of his own essential defectiveness rather than as the random cruelty it is), and a nascent **should-statement morality** absorbed from Ben's gentle didacticism and May's quiet anxiety.

**Self-concept.** Stably negative in the social/embodied register; stably positive but unvoiced in the intellectual register. He knows he is smart. He does not yet know he is allowed to be liked. The split is pre-Spider-Man; the costume only later gives it a name.

**Attachment.** Anxious-preoccupied with caregiving inversion already detectable — he monitors May's health, regulates around Ben's moods, modulates his school complaints to spare them worry. This is the **parentified child** profile, and it is the soil from which the responsibility schema will later grow.

---

## II. THE ORIGINATING FRACTURE AND ITS FIRST FIVE YEARS (AF #15 → ASM ~#38; subject age ~15–18)

**Affect regulation — acute phase.** The week of Ben's murder establishes the lifelong somatic template: grief is metabolized through **motor discharge** (the chase, the warehouse confrontation) followed by **isolation of affect** (the silent walk home in the final panel, the famous receding figure). Tears are private. Within months he has installed the regulatory architecture that will persist sixty years: **patter as in-vivo affect modulation**. The early Ditko-era quips are awkward, almost forced — a teenager rehearsing a defense — but the function is already clear. Joke density rises with threat. The fight commentary is not bravado; it is the same self-soothing that humming serves for a frightened child, externalized into language because language is what he has.

**Cognitive style — distortion installation.** Beck's catalogue is present in nearly pure form within twelve months of the bite: **personalization** ("the burglar I let pass killed Ben — therefore Ben's death is *my* act"), **should-statements** ("I *should* have stopped him; I *must* now stop all of them"), **emotional reasoning** ("I feel guilty, therefore I am guilty"), and **disqualifying the positive** (every save is necessary baseline, no save is credit). The Master Planner sequence (ASM #31–33) is the first behavioral X-ray of the cognitive architecture: under the rubble, the inner monologue passes through despair → self-recrimination → reframe to duty-toward-dependent → motor breakthrough. The reframe is the load-bearing step, and it is *cognitive*, not affective. He does not feel better; he feels obligated, and obligation is what moves the rubble.

**Self-concept.** Bifurcation begins. "Peter" — failing socially, exhausted, broke, lying to May — accrues most of the negative valence; "Spider-Man" becomes the container for whatever competence he can acknowledge. The Jameson campaign is, perversely, *integrated* into this structure: the public defamation confirms his negative self-image while letting him fund the maternal household, satisfying both the masochism and the duty.

**Attachment.** Caregiving inversion goes total with respect to May. He becomes her co-parent, financial provider, and emotional stabilizer simultaneously, all while concealing the role that consumes his life. The first romantic approaches (Betty Brant, Liz Allan) display the pattern that will never resolve: **approach → intensification → withdrawal at the threshold of true vulnerability**, always rationalized through external constraint (a call to action, a need to lie about whereabouts). The constraint is real; the relief it provides from intimacy-dread is also real.

---

## III. COLLEGE AND CATASTROPHE (ASM #39 → ~#150; subject age ~18–22)

**Affect regulation — broadening and brittling.** The Romita-era expansion of his social world (Gwen, MJ, Harry, Flash humanized) gives him more affect to regulate and more rehearsed regulatory strategies. Humor matures — it is no longer rehearsed, it is fluent. He begins to display genuine affective warmth in non-mission contexts (the early Gwen romance, the Harry friendship). But the regulatory range above and below a narrow center remains shallow: he cannot tolerate sustained joy without anticipating its withdrawal, and he cannot tolerate sustained grief without intellectualizing it into mission.

**The Captain Stacy event (ASM #90)** introduces the first **trauma-laminated reactivation**: the death recapitulates Ben's, the deathbed transfer of responsibility ("be good to her") recapitulates the Ben schema in explicit verbal form. Affect-regulation in the aftermath is *not* grief-work; it is concealment. He cannot tell Gwen the truth and so cannot mourn with her.

**The Gwen event (ASM #121).** This is the structural fulcrum of the entire psychological profile. Janoff-Bulman's "shattered assumptions" framework applies almost diagrammatically: the assumptions that *the world is benevolent*, that *the self is competent*, and that *outcomes are contingent on effort* are all violated in a single act in which his **competent saving move kills the beloved**. Pre-Gwen, the schema was *I must act to prevent harm*. Post-Gwen, the schema mutates to *my action may itself be the harm*, generating a permanent **intimacy-as-hazard** overlay. The behavioral footprint is immediate and durable: hesitancy in subsequent rescues of loved ones (the half-second of paralysis observable in pencils across decades), the substitution of webbing-architecture redundancy for direct catch when possible, and — interpersonally — the introduction of a **withdrawal-at-deepening** pattern absent from the pre-Gwen romance.

**The brief homicidal-rage sequence post-Gwen** (the confrontation with Norman, ASM #122) is the first observable **acting-out breakthrough**. It is short, it is followed by remorse, and it is sealed off — but it is real, and it tells the file that under sufficient load the conscience can be overrun. He will spend the rest of his life ensuring this does not recur.

**Cognitive style.** Convergent problem-solving remains dominant; **catastrophic counterfactual rumination** is newly installed and never leaves ("if I had webbed her differently…"). The Jackal/clone arc (ASM #149) introduces **ontological anxiety** as a permanent low-frequency hum: am I the original? — a question that under stress will recruit every other doubt he carries.

**Self-concept.** The Peter/Spider-Man split deepens, with Spider-Man now also carrying the wound of having-killed. He treats Spider-Man less as the functional self and more as the *condemned* self — the one whose hands have done damage. Peter, by contrast, becomes the part that *deserves* the punishment of being Spider-Man.

**Attachment.** Re-stabilizes around MJ in a relationship that survives precisely because she, uniquely, perceives the split and tolerates the withdrawal-at-threshold without taking it as rejection. The friendship-then-romance arc is **earned secure attachment in vivo**, the closest he comes to corrective experience.

---

## IV. THE STERN/DEFALCO YEARS — COMPULSIVE CONSOLIDATION (late 70s–mid 80s; subject mid-20s)

**Affect regulation.** Stabilizes into the **adult signature**: humor + sublimation + intellectualization as a tightly integrated suite, with brief regressions under specific triggers (Burglar's return, ASM #200; Hobgoblin identity-paranoia). The "Nothing Can Stop the Juggernaut" arc (ASM #229–230) is the behavioral apotheosis of **affect-overridden duty execution**: he gets up because no one else will, and the rising-up is not courage in the felt sense — it is the responsibility schema running as autonomic procedure. Fear is present; it is simply not allowed steering authority.

**Cognitive style.** Adds **mission decomposition** as a habit: he breaks impossible problems into solvable sub-problems and works the sub-problems even when the meta-problem is hopeless. This is adaptive in combat and engineering; it is *maladaptive* in his interior life, where it lets him work the sub-problems of patrol and bills while leaving the meta-problem (his unprocessed grief) untouched indefinitely.

**Self-concept.** The "loser" framing solidifies into an identity-stable joke he tells about himself with a half-smile. Vaillant would code this as **mature humor with a substrate of self-deprecation that functions defensively** — it preempts external criticism by interiorizing it first.

---

## V. THE SYMBIOTE / KRAVEN / MARRIAGE ERA (ASM #252–300, Annual #21, Kraven's Last Hunt; late 20s)

**Affect regulation — under exogenous compromise.** The symbiote episode is, clinically, an **involuntary disinhibition experiment** on a subject whose entire personality structure is built around inhibition. The amplified aggression and the nocturnal patrols-without-memory are not him; but the *relief* of having something else carry the load is something he can recognize, and the recognition frightens him into severance. The clinical residue is twofold: (a) a **calibrated terror of any altered-state experience** (the lifelong abstinence from alcohol and sedatives is reinforced here), and (b) a small but real **awareness that the load he carries is, in fact, too heavy** — an awareness he will spend the next decades re-suppressing.

**Kraven's Last Hunt.** Criterion-A trauma in textbook form: actual death (he is shot, he is *believed dead*), prolonged entrapment (~two weeks buried), forced helplessness, identity violation (Kraven wears the suit and commits acts in his name). The post-event behavior is **dissociative continuation**: he digs out, he resumes patrol within days, he does not tell MJ the full shape of what happened, he does not seek even informal support. This is **isolation of affect** in its most somatic form — the experience is filed in a part of the self that does not communicate with the part that lives the life. Anniversary-effect intrusions across subsequent decades (panel cues to dirt, confinement, the specific shovel-imagery) confirm that the material was never processed, only sequestered.

**Marriage to MJ.** Functions as a **corrective attachment experiment** of significant duration. The MJ relationship, when it is healthy, supplies the only sustained interpersonal context in which Peter is *seen* — costume off, schema and all — and not destroyed by the seeing. The clinical relevance is that the relationship *demonstrates his capacity for secure-base behavior when a partner is willing to absorb the withdrawal-at-threshold pattern without retaliation*. The data point is important: the dysfunction is not characterological-immutable; it is schema-driven, and the schema responds to corrective experience when the experience is sustained.

**Self-concept.** Marriage briefly admits a third frame beyond "Peter the loser" and "Spider-Man the condemned" — **"Peter the husband,"** a frame in which he is chosen rather than tolerated. The frame is fragile and will be repeatedly attacked.

---

## VI. THE CLONE SAGA AND ITS SEQUELAE (1994–1996; subject ~30)

**Affect regulation — under ontological assault.** When the narrative tells him he is the clone, the reaction is not the rage one would expect from a narcissistically organized personality; it is a **quiet relinquishment**. He walks away. He lets the "original" be Spider-Man. He tries to live a civilian life with a pregnant MJ. The relinquishment is diagnostically rich: it reveals that **a part of him has been waiting decades for permission to stop**, and that the permission-condition he has set is impossibly high (not "I am tired" but "I am not the real one"). The brief civilian interval is the only sustained data we have on what his nervous system does when the role is removed — and it does not do well. Restlessness, hypervigilance without object, a sense of unmooring. The role is so deeply integrated that its absence is itself dysregulating.

**Cognitive style.** **Identity-paranoia** as a low-grade chronic feature, reactivated and intensified.

**Self-concept.** Briefly destabilized to the point of dissolution, then re-cohered around the role. The episode demonstrates the **role-as-scaffold**: take the role away and the self is not free, the self is *collapsing*.

---

## VII. JMS / TOTEMIC / CIVIL WAR / ONE MORE DAY (2001–2007; subject mid-30s)

**Affect regulation — partial maturation, catastrophic compromise.** The JMS years depict a Peter who, in the teaching of high school students, accesses a Ben-position for the first time at scale — the **reparative caregiving** that is, in this profile, his most consistently healing activity. There is genuine adult settledness in this period. May's discovery of the identity (ASM vol.2 #38) and her acceptance of it is corrective at the deepest schema-level: the maternal figure *knows* and *does not break*. For a brief window, the responsibility schema is contested by lived experience.

**Civil War.** The public unmasking is the most consequential **regulatory failure** of his adult life. Behaviorally: a man whose entire operational architecture has been compartmentalization, performed on national television in a state of disrupted judgment driven by **paternal transference to Stark**. The transference is itself diagnostic — he is so attachment-hungry for a competent father-figure that he overrides decades of operant learning to please one. The defection that follows is consistent with the conscience-primacy of his structure, but the damage is irrevocable: May is shot.

**One More Day.** Whatever the editorial provenance, the *behavior* is fully consistent with the schema: confronted with a mother-figure dying on his watch as a consequence of his own catastrophic judgment, he will pay any cost — including the marriage that was his single most corrective relationship — to prevent the loss. The decision is **the responsibility schema in its terminal form**: rather than tolerate the recurrence of the originating wound, he sacrifices the relationship that was healing it. The clinical reading is bleak: the schema is willing to consume the very mechanism that could revise it.

---

## VIII. SLOTT / SUPERIOR / PARKER INDUSTRIES (2008–2018; subject ~40)

**Affect regulation — post-OMD reset and the Octavius interval.** Returns to bachelor precarity with affective signatures of grief he cannot consciously name (the marriage is gone in a way his memory does not fully account for; the residue is a low chronic ache and an inhibition around MJ that he reads as ordinary loss). Humor remains intact; depth slightly diminished — there is a faintly more brittle quality to the patter in this period.

**The Superior interval** is an unprecedented psychiatric event: a **dissociative non-analog** in which executive control is occupied by another consciousness while his own observes. The post-restoration self is fractionally different — slightly more strategic, marginally more willing to delegate, with newly inserted memories of Octavius's choices that he must integrate. Clinically: he integrates them by treating them as a kind of loaned competence he is obliged to redeem ethically. There is no observable identity confusion; there is a subtle widening of his repertoire.

**Parker Industries.** A behavioral experiment in **inhabiting success**. He cannot. The collapse is over-determined — narrative villainy plays its role — but the *characterological* contribution is unmistakable: he sabotages comfort because the schema does not allow him to occupy a station in which he is not suffering for others. The return to working-class precarity is, at the schema level, **ego-syntonic relief**. He is back where he believes he belongs.

**Self-concept.** Slightly more integrated than at any prior point. The Spider-Family — Miles, the various Spiders he mentors — supplies a **generative Eriksonian frame** he had previously accessed only piecemeal. Caregiving outward to younger heroes is the most durable repair mechanism in his adult life because it lets him *be Ben for someone else*, which is the only undoing the schema actually accepts.

---

## IX. SPENCER / WELLS AND THE PRESENT (2018–present; subject ~40+)

**Affect regulation.** Stable in shape, slightly more weathered in tone. The Kindred (Harry) arc re-litigates the Osborn wound with characteristic effect: prior losses are reactivated as a stack rather than processed individually. The humor remains; the eyes behind it (in the textual interior) are tireder.

**Cognitive style.** Largely unchanged in structure. The personalization-and-should distortions remain load-bearing. There is, however, a small accumulating wisdom — a willingness, sometimes, to *name* the schema in interior monologue ("of course I think it's my fault, I always think it's my fault") that did not exist in earlier decades. This is **meta-cognitive awareness without behavioral change** — a stage that, in clinical work, often precedes change by years. The file should note it as a positive prognostic indicator.

**Self-concept.** The three frames — deficient civilian, condemned hero, generative mentor — coexist with increasing fluidity. The mentor frame is gaining proportional weight. If the longitudinal trajectory continues, the next decade should show further migration of self-investment from the condemned-hero frame toward the generative-mentor frame, with corresponding reduction in self-punishment intensity.

---

## X. SYNTHESIS — WHAT EVOLVED, WHAT DID NOT

**Evolved.**
- Humor: from rehearsed to fluent to weathered, with consistent affect-regulatory function but increasing relational warmth.
- Mentorship capacity: from absent (he was too young) to incidental to central. The single clearest growth axis.
- Meta-cognitive awareness of his own schema: from zero to partial, articulated in recent interior monologue.
- Tolerance for sustained intimacy: increased during MJ marriage, regressed post-OMD, slowly recovering.
- Strategic patience in combat: increased post-Superior.

**Did not evolve, or evolved minimally.**
- The responsibility schema itself — personalization, should-statements, undoing — remains load-bearing across sixty years.
- Somatic self-neglect — sleep, nutrition, refusal of medical and psychological care — unchanged.
- Withdrawal-at-threshold in romantic intimacy — recurs across every romantic partner.
- Intimacy-as-hazard overlay from the Gwen event — persistent.
- Class/comfort intolerance — he cannot rest in success.

**Prognosis, longitudinal.** The structure is unusually durable because it is **ego-syntonic and prosocially reinforced**: the schema produces behavior the world rewards, which prevents the dysphoria-threshold necessary to motivate change. Absent a catastrophic disruption (which his life supplies regularly, with no curative effect) or a sustained corrective relationship of sufficient duration to override the schema (the MJ marriage approached this and was undone), revision is unlikely to occur spontaneously. The most plausible vector of slow positive change is the **mentor frame**: each young hero who survives and thrives under his guidance is a small piece of evidence against the proposition that proximity to him is lethal. Over decades, the accumulated evidence may, finally, begin to revise the schema's central claim.

The file's working assessment: a subject of extraordinary structural stability, persistent sub-clinical suffering, durable prosocial output, and a slow, late-emerging capacity for self-recognition that is the first genuine grounds for hope the record has produced.


## Psychiatric Assessment & Differential

# PSYCHIATRIC ASSESSMENT & DIFFERENTIAL — SUBJECT: PARKER, PETER B.

*Assessment-by-record. The subject has, to UATU's knowledge, never sat for formal psychiatric evaluation. The closest approaches — Dr. Ashley Kafka's incidental encounters, Dr. Andrea Janson (compromised), Dr. Faustus (adversarial), Madame Web's quasi-therapeutic presence, and a single brief court-mandated counseling sleeve during the early Slott run — were each terminated or refused before any standardized instrument could be administered. What follows is therefore a behavior-record assessment, conducted to clinical standards of formulation but without the corroboration any responsible clinician would demand.*

---

## I. PRESENTING SIGNATURE

If the subject walked into an outpatient intake at age 33 (where the published record approximately stabilizes him) and were honest — a counterfactual; he would not be — the chief complaints organized from observable behavior would read approximately:

1. Chronic sleep insufficiency (4–5 hours, fragmented, with frequent forcible waking by hypervigilant arousal events he can no longer disentangle from genuine threat signal).
2. Persistent intrusive imagery, primarily of three discrete scenes: the Acme Warehouse unmasking of the burglar; Gwen Stacy's final fall and the crack at the bottom of the line; the moment of recognizing his own body in motion, performed by another, during the Octavius occupation.
3. Anhedonic baseline, masked, with episodic deepening that the subject describes (in interior monologue across writers) as "bad weeks" or "the gray."
4. Relationship instability framed as external misfortune but reported with a constancy that suggests internal patterning.
5. Compulsive overcommitment of time and physical resources to an unpaid second occupation he experiences as non-optional.
6. Somatic complaints he will not articulate: chronic lumbar and cervical pain, tinnitus of moderate severity, intermittent paresthesias in the dominant hand, gastric symptoms consistent with under-eating-then-binging cycles.

The presentation he would *offer* would be cheerful, self-deprecating, and laden with humor calibrated to make the clinician laugh and discharge him. The discrepancy between the offered presentation and the inferable internal state is itself a diagnostic datum of the first order.

---

## II. PRIMARY DIAGNOSES (DSM-5-TR / ICD-11 ANALOGS)

### A. Posttraumatic Stress Disorder, chronic, with delayed expression and recurrent exacerbations (DSM-5-TR 309.81 / ICD-11 6B40)

**The strongest-supported diagnosis on the record, and the one that organizes most else.**

*Criterion A — exposure.* Vastly over-met. Index event: discovery of Benjamin Parker's corpse and subsequent identification of the killer as the man he had failed to stop, occurring at approximately age 15, with the additional traumatogenic feature of personal omission. Secondary index-class events, each individually criterion-A qualifying: George Stacy's death in his arms (ASM #90); Gwen Stacy's death by mechanical action of his own webline (ASM #121); the Kraven entrapment (shot, buried alive ~two weeks, exhumation by self-effort with no recovery interval) — a textbook compound criterion-A event combining mortal threat, prolonged confinement, and post-event isolation; Harry Osborn's death; Aunt May's repeated near-deaths and the false-death of ASM #400; the symbiote bonding and rejection sequence; Civil War unmasking and consequences; the Octavius body-occupation. The traumatic load is *cumulative*, *relational*, and *identity-implicating* — a profile that the trauma literature recognizes as among the most pathogenic configurations possible.

*Criterion B — intrusion.* Documented in interior monologue with cross-decade consistency. Gwen-flashbacks recur at moments of falling and of catching, indexed to the somatosensory cue of a body decelerating on a line. The unmasked-burglar image surfaces in moments of moral hesitation. The Kraven-coffin imagery returns under confinement, under sensory deprivation, and — diagnostically interesting — under any felt loss of agency. Nightmare content depicted across runs is consistent with the index events. He has dissociative-flashback episodes (DSM B3) during specific combat triggers, most reliably when an opponent uses a falling-bystander hostage tactic.

*Criterion C — avoidance.* Behavioral, not stated. He does not walk past the George Washington Bridge tower from which Gwen fell when he can route around it; published swing-routes from his apartments to Manhattan consistently bias east of the canonical site. He has not, on record, willingly returned to the Acme Warehouse. May 6 (variable canon for Ben's death anniversary) is depicted as a withdrawal day. He avoids the topic of Gwen with surviving connections (Mary Jane, in particular) using humor and subject-change.

*Criterion D — negative cognitions and mood.* Persistent and exaggerated negative beliefs about self ("I should have stopped him"; "everyone I love ends up hurt") — these are not occasional intrusive thoughts but a stable self-narrative, and they meet criterion D2 ("persistent distorted cognitions about the cause or consequences of the traumatic event") in textbook form. Persistent negative emotional state (guilt, shame, fear) is the dysthymic substrate beneath the humor. Diminished interest in significant activities is episodic but real (the post-Gwen withdrawal from photography, the periodic abandonments of academic work). Feelings of detachment from others — concealed behind warmth, but evident in the systematic non-disclosure even to intimates.

*Criterion E — arousal and reactivity.* This is the criterion where his clinical picture is *biologically* confounded. The spider-sense produces a hypervigilance signal that an ordinary clinician would code as criterion E3. In his case the signal is partially veridical — there really are threats — but the behavioral response (constant scanning, startle on novel auditory stimulus even when the spider-sense has *not* fired, inability to sit with his back to a door or window, the consistent rooftop perch with full sightlines) is amplified well beyond what the prosthetic threat-sense requires. Sleep disturbance, irritability under fatigue, reckless or self-destructive behavior (the willingness to take fights with negative expected outcomes) — all met.

*Course.* The diagnosis is chronic with delayed expression (criterion specifier met by the consistent observation that immediate post-Ben behavior was action-oriented and the depressive/intrusive features deepened over months and years). Exacerbations are predictably tied to anniversary effects and to new losses, with each new criterion-A event reactivating the symptom stack from all prior events — the *kindling pattern* characteristic of repeatedly traumatized populations.

### B. Persistent Depressive Disorder (DSM-5-TR 300.4 / ICD-11 6A72), with intermittent Major Depressive Episodes

The dysthymic substrate is the most consistently legible affective feature across sixty years of interior monologue. The depressed mood is present more days than not, by his own narration, masked from external observers by humor. Of the six DSM criterion-B features, the record supports at least four chronically: poor appetite or overeating (the erratic-then-binge nutrition pattern), insomnia (chronic and over-determined), low energy (denied, but inferable from the consistent depiction of dragging himself to patrol), low self-esteem (overwhelming and continuous), and feelings of hopelessness (episodic but recurrent, particularly post-loss). Duration vastly exceeds the two-year threshold.

Superimposed Major Depressive Episodes — meeting full criteria, with five-plus symptoms over two-plus weeks and functional impairment — are observable in discrete post-loss periods: the months after Gwen, the post-Kraven recovery (his functioning is depicted as preserved on the surface, but the interior is consistent with MDE), the Harry Osborn aftermath, the One-More-Day-adjacent grief period, the immediate post-Octavius return when he must reckon with the actions taken in his body. The DSM specifier *with anxious distress* applies essentially continuously; the specifier *with melancholic features* applies in the deeper troughs (early-morning waking, anhedonia, excessive guilt).

### C. Complex Posttraumatic Stress Disorder (ICD-11 6B41) — supported

ICD-11 CPTSD requires all PTSD criteria plus three additional *disturbances in self-organization*: (1) affective dysregulation, (2) negative self-concept, and (3) interpersonal disturbances. All three are present with longitudinal stability.

*Affective dysregulation* manifests in his case at the *under-regulated* end (occasional rage breakthroughs followed by self-punishment) and far more often at the *over-regulated* end (the humor-armored isolation of affect, the somatic dissociation under acute load — Kraven aftermath, symbiote period — where feeling is shunted out of conscious access to permit continued role performance).

*Negative self-concept* is the through-line of his interior life. He believes he is fundamentally insufficient — as a provider, as a partner, as a nephew/son, as a hero — and no quantity of contradicting evidence revises the belief. This is not a momentary cognition; it is a stable schema.

*Interpersonal disturbances* take the specific form of attachment-with-sabotage. He pursues intimacy and undermines it at the threshold where loss would become unbearable, then experiences the resulting failure as confirmation of his unsuitability.

The CPTSD frame is, in this clinician's view, a *more accurate* description of the subject than PTSD alone, because it captures the developmental-temporal dimension (his trauma history spans adolescence into middle adulthood and is relationally embedded) that DSM PTSD does not fully accommodate.

### D. Obsessive-Compulsive Personality features, subclinical / accentuated, scrupulous variant (DSM-5-TR — does not meet full PD threshold)

The over-responsibility, the moralized perfectionism, the inability to delegate without anxiety, the conviction that rest is moral failure, the rigid ethical scrupulosity (the no-kill rule held even at predictable cost), the workaholic absorption that crowds out leisure and relationships — these are textbook OCPD features in the scrupulous-moral variant. He does not meet the full disorder threshold because (a) his cognitive flexibility within problem domains is high; he is not rigid about *means*, only about *ends*; (b) he is generous with material resources rather than miserly; (c) interpersonal warmth is preserved. The features are accentuated, not disordered, but they do real damage.

### E. Specific anxiety-spectrum features

Generalized anxiety baseline is present, though under-diagnosable separately given the PTSD frame absorbs most of the variance. Specific phobic-strength avoidance of two stimuli is observable: (1) confined spaces with restricted air — the Kraven legacy, the only specific phobia (DSM 300.29) he displays with full criterion-meeting intensity, manifesting in startle, sweating, tachycardia, and avoidance of basements, sealed chambers, and earth-walled spaces; (2) the sensation of a falling body decelerating against a line he is holding — a more contextual but extremely reliable trigger.

### F. Acute Stress / dissociative episodes — historical, discrete

Symbiote bonding (3–4 weeks of altered consciousness and impaired volitional control); post-Kraven re-emergence (days of derealization and isolation of affect); Octavius occupation (months of observer-self experience in own body — a presentation with no clean DSM analog, closest perhaps to a forced depersonalization-derealization state of unprecedented duration and concrete cause). Each is historical, not ongoing, but each leaves residue: the symbiote period sensitized him to any felt loss of agency; the Octavius period left an undischarged horror that his body itself can become an instrument used against the people he loves.

---

## III. ETIOLOGY — A FOUR-FACTOR FORMULATION

**Predisposing factors.** Early parental loss (ages indeterminate but pre-school, per retconned record), generating baseline attachment anxiety and an internal working model in which beloved figures disappear. Adoption by elderly caregivers, intensifying anticipatory mourning by demographic fact. Intellectually gifted, socially isolated temperament — bullied, lunch-alone, refuge-in-books — generating a self-concept of *not belonging among ordinary people* that pre-dates and prefigures the secret-identity structure. Pre-bite somatic frailty contributing to a body-image of insufficiency that the bite alters mechanically but does not heal psychologically.

**Precipitating factor.** The Ben Parker murder, with the specific feature that the subject *had had the opportunity to prevent it* via a refused prosocial act minutes earlier. This is the *ideal pathogenic configuration* for chronic guilt: a discrete event, externally consequential, traceable to a single morally-coded omission, occurring during peak adolescent identity formation, with no possibility of redress. The "great power, great responsibility" cognition formed in the immediate aftermath functions thereafter as a *core schema* in the Beckian sense — a self-relevant generalization that filters subsequent experience.

**Perpetuating factors.** A moral framework that re-encodes guilt as virtue, removing the motivation to revise the schema. Social and operational roles (Spider-Man, breadwinner-for-May, mentor) that demand the perpetuation of the over-responsible stance. Repeated traumatic exposure without recovery intervals — by canonical patrol frequency he sustains a new minor criterion-A-adjacent event most weeks. Absence of any clinical, religious, or peer-supervisory structure that could interrupt the loop. Financial precarity functioning as an additional stressor and as ongoing confirmation of inadequacy. Identity secrecy preventing the kind of disclosure that would permit ordinary social support to operate on the trauma material.

**Protective factors.** High intelligence (provides instrumental competence and cognitive flexibility within problem domains). Humor, deployed with skill, generating real affect-regulation and real interpersonal connection. Sustained — if turbulent — attachments to a small core (May, Mary Jane in some configurations, a handful of hero-peers). Prosocial role with genuine consequential utility, producing reality-grounded self-efficacy that buffers the schema-driven self-attack. Mentorship reciprocity (Miles Morales, the Spider-Family configurations) which permits him to occupy the Ben-position for others — a reparative arrangement of considerable therapeutic value even though informally arranged. Absence of substance use as self-medication, which would otherwise compound the picture severely.

---

## IV. COMORBIDITY MAP

The diagnostic features are not independent; they constitute a *coherent syndrome* in which trauma sequelae, depressive substrate, anxious arousal, and personality-level over-responsibility mutually reinforce one another. Treating any one in isolation would predictably fail. The CPTSD frame integrates the PTSD, dysthymic, and OCPD-trait dimensions into a single longitudinal picture; the discrete phobic features and the historical dissociative episodes attach as event-specific outgrowths. The somatic neglect is a *behavioral consequence* of the psychiatric picture, not an independent diagnosis, but it generates real medical morbidity that loops back into mood and arousal regulation.

---

## V. COURSE OVER TIME

*Adolescence (15–18).* Acute post-traumatic onset, masked by action-orientation. School performance preserved, social functioning marginal-to-impaired. Sleep disturbance and intrusive imagery established. First episodes of operational depression.

*Early adulthood (18–25).* Dysthymic baseline consolidates. Romantic engagement begins; first major loss (Gwen) re-traumatizes and adds the closeness-is-dangerous overlay to the attachment system. Captain Stacy's death precedes and primes. Repeated lower-grade traumas accumulate without intervention. Humor as defense matures from adolescent deflection to skilled affect-regulation.

*Mid-adulthood (25–35).* Kraven entrapment marks the high-water mark of acute trauma exposure with the most severe acute-stress sequelae. Marriage period offers genuine protective gain — the dysthymic baseline lifts measurably during stable MJ periods, which is itself a strong diagnostic confirmation that the depression is partly relationally responsive. Symbiote period introduces the agency-loss vulnerability. Identity disclosure (Civil War) and subsequent maternal-figure crisis produce a moral-coherence rupture that, in this clinician's reading, the subject has never fully repaired.

*Later (35–present).* Continued cycling. The Octavius occupation introduces a horror substrate that the record does not show him processing. Mentorship of younger heroes provides real reparative benefit. Class-and-identity rigidity (the failed transition to Stark-scale success) demonstrates that the schema now constrains *upward* mobility as actively as it once constrained *downward* protection. Anniversary effects appear to be intensifying with age and trauma load.

*Prognosis without intervention.* Stable chronic course with predictable acute exacerbations on each new loss. No spontaneous remission likely; the perpetuating factors are too structurally embedded. Mortality risk via passive death-acceptance is real but moderate, buffered by attachment commitments. Somatic morbidity from cumulative trauma load and chronic neglect is the more probable cause of premature loss of function.

*Prognosis with intervention.* Treatable, in principle, with sustained trauma-focused work (the trauma material is well-defined, the cognitive distortions are well-formed enough to be addressable in cognitive therapy, the affective range is preserved). The barriers are entirely structural: identity secrecy preventing honest disclosure to any standard provider; operational tempo precluding consistent attendance; *and* — most fundamentally — the patient's own conviction that his suffering is morally required.

---

## VI. RIGOROUS DIFFERENTIAL — WHAT HE IS NOT, AND WHY

The diagnostic clarity of this case depends on as much being said about what the record *excludes* as about what it supports. Each of the following has been or could be casually attached to the subject; each is wrong, for specific evidentiary reasons.

**Not Narcissistic Personality Disorder.** The diagnosis requires a pervasive pattern of grandiosity, need for admiration, and lack of empathy. The subject's self-evaluation is consistently and pervasively negative; he does not seek admiration and is visibly uncomfortable when offered it (the recurring refusal of public credit, the deflection of thanks); his empathy is *over*-developed to a degree that itself causes morbidity. The costumed identity is not a grandiose self-presentation but a functional disguise behind which he conceals what he believes to be the real, deficient self. The diagnosis is excluded.

**Not Antisocial Personality Disorder, nor any psychopathy variant.** Conscience is the subject's *defining feature* and the engine of his pathology, not its absence. Remorse is excessive, not deficient. There is no history of deceit for personal gain (the identity concealment is protective, not exploitative), no impulsivity in the antisocial sense, no aggressive disregard for others' welfare — quite the inverse. Excluded categorically.

**Not Bipolar Disorder, either type.** No hypomanic or manic episodes meeting duration or symptom criteria appear in the record. Energy fluctuations track sleep deficit, crisis demand, and depressive trough — they are *exogenous*, not endogenous-cyclical. Goal-directed activity is chronically elevated but in a sustained workaholic pattern, not in discrete elevated episodes. Sleep need is reduced situationally, never as a primary symptom of mood elevation. Grandiosity absent. Pressured speech absent (the humor is patter, not pressure — it is intentional, modulated, and stops when ineffective). Excluded.

**Not Schizoid Personality Disorder.** The diagnosis requires detachment from social relationships and a restricted range of expressed emotion. The subject *desires* and *pursues* intimacy with great intensity; his avoidance is conflict- and fear-driven, not pleasure-deficient. Affective range is wide and expressive. Excluded.

**Not Schizotypal or any psychotic-spectrum disorder.** Reality-testing is preserved across the record. The spider-sense is a veridical perceptual augmentation, not a hallucination — it tracks real external referents reliably enough to be empirically validated by outcomes. No formal thought disorder, no delusions, no negative symptoms. The unusual experiences (totemic spider mythology, contact with cosmic entities) are *consensus realities* in his universe, not idiosyncratic beliefs. Excluded.

**Not Avoidant Personality Disorder.** Though shy and self-critical, the subject does not avoid occupational or interpersonal contact requiring significant interpersonal contact; quite the contrary. He is socially inhibited only in narrow relational domains and *only* about specific concealed material; in his public-facing operational identity he is voluble, engaging, and proactive. The criterion-level pervasiveness is absent. Excluded.

**Not Dependent Personality Disorder.** He bears the entire decision-load of his moral and operational life independently, often to a fault. Reliance on others is something he actively resists, sometimes destructively. Excluded.

**Not Dissociative Identity Disorder.** The Peter/Spider-Man distinction is *role differentiation* with full memory continuity, a single executive self, and no amnestic gaps between presentations. He is the same person in both modes; he wears different clothes and uses different vocal calibrations. The Octavius episode was a third party physically occupying his body, not an alter — it is categorically a different phenomenon and arguably warranted a separate diagnostic line (forced depersonalization-derealization under exogenous control) which is what we have given it. DID excluded.

**Not Borderline Personality Disorder.** No identity diffusion in the BPD sense — his identity is *over*-coherent, the same self-concept across decades and contexts. No splitting in object relations; his perceptions of significant others are nuanced and stable. No chronic emptiness. No frantic abandonment-avoidance acts; if anything, he initiates separations to *prevent* abandonment-by-death of the other. No self-harm of the BPD type, though the passive death-acceptance has some functional overlap. Excluded.

**Not Histrionic Personality Disorder, and not "martyr complex" in the attention-seeking sense.** The sacrifices are *concealed*. He hides costs from the people they benefit. There is no theatricality, no need to be the center of attention; the patter is in fact *anti-attention* — it deflects scrutiny by signaling unseriousness. The martyr pattern is internally guilt-driven, not externally display-driven. Excluded.

**Not Generalized Anxiety Disorder as primary.** The anxiety is present and pervasive but is better accounted for by the PTSD/CPTSD frame as


## Behavioral Atlas

# BEHAVIORAL ATLAS — SUBJECT PARKER, P. B.

*Compiled from longitudinal panel-level observation, 1962–present. The unit of analysis is the micro-behavior: posture, latency, verbal tic, breath, gait, sequencing under stimulus. What follows is the operational manual a watcher would need to predict him within thirty seconds of contact.*

---

## I. BASELINE — THE CALM STATE (Rare; ~ 4–9% of observed waking hours)

True baseline is anomalous in this subject and should be flagged when observed. It occurs in narrow windows: late mornings after rare full sleep, in May Parker's kitchen, on rooftops at dawn pre-patrol, in laboratory absorption when a problem is going well, and in the first three minutes of a successful date before vigilance returns.

**Postural signature.** Habitually rounded thoracic kyphosis from years of microscope, monitor, and webslinging hunch — but in calm states the shoulders descend visibly, a drop of perhaps two centimeters at the acromion. He leans. Forearms on tables, shoulder against doorframes, hip cocked against counters. The musculature does not fully relax — it never does — but the *recruitment pattern* shifts from braced to draped.

**Hands.** At rest, the right hand often performs a slow, half-conscious pad-to-pad finger walk: index–middle–ring–pinkie–reverse, like a pianist warming or a man counting prime factors. When this stops mid-cycle, he has noticed something.

**Face.** Resting expression is mild, slightly amused, mouth closed with a small asymmetric lift at the right corner — a residual smirk that costs him nothing to wear. Eyes are quick-scanning even at rest: a small saccadic survey of the room every fifteen to twenty-five seconds, which he himself does not register as vigilance.

**Voice.** Pitched in a comfortable mid-tenor, with a Queens-inflected vowel set that broadens slightly when he is at ease (the "cawfee" / "tawk" register he otherwise suppresses in professional settings). Cadence unhurried; sentences complete; jokes still present but lower in density — perhaps one bit per ninety seconds rather than one per fifteen.

**Eating.** Calm eating is identifiable by *pace*. He chews. He puts the fork down between bites. Under stress he shovels. At Aunt May's table specifically he will accept seconds without being asked twice, an unusually compliant micro-behavior for him.

**The tell that calm is ending.** A small breath in through the nose, held for a half-beat, released through a barely parted mouth. If you see this and his right hand stops mid-finger-walk, he has heard, felt, or *intuited* something a quarter-second before anyone else in the room. Begin counting; he will be moving within four seconds.

---

## II. THE WORK STATE — LABORATORY / WORKBENCH ABSORPTION

A distinct mode, neither calm nor stressed; it is the closest thing he has to meditation.

**Setup ritual.** Tools arranged in a left-to-right cascade by frequency of anticipated use. Coffee placed at upper right of the bench, never centered. Phone face-down at upper left.
