**Condition C — Withdrawal or compromise of a primary attachment figure.** When May is hospitalized, MJ is estranged, and the Spider-Family is geographically scattered, his stage-3-to-4 transition accelerates because the people who would normally interrupt the cycle by *noticing* are unavailable. The protective effect of these relationships is not advice — he rarely accepts advice — but *witnessing*. To be seen at stage 2 by someone who knows him is to be returned to stage 1 by the encounter itself. Without witnesses, the descent accelerates.

**Condition D — A frame offered by an authority-coded or paternal-coded figure that promises to resolve the unbearable.** The accelerant for Type A rupture. The Stark figure during Civil War; the symbiote, framed as a costume gift; Mephisto, framed as a being who can simply lift the consequence. Note that the figure need not be trustworthy — the historical record shows him accepting frames from figures he intellectually distrusts when the stage-5 state has eroded the gating. **Adversaries who have understood this — Norman Osborn primarily, Octavius secondarily, Kraven through ritual rather than offer — have been able to engineer his collapse far more efficiently than those who simply attack.**

All four conditions co-present produce, with high reliability, a stage-5 event within days to weeks. Three of four produce it within months. Two of four produce sustained stage-4 with intermittent stage-3 recovery. One of four is absorbed by baseline defenses.

---

## 6.4 SIGNATURE FAILURE PATTERNS BY DOMAIN

**Combat decompensation.** Under stage-3 and above, he develops a recognizable late-fight signature: he stops disengaging when disengagement is tactically indicated. Standard Parker combat doctrine is hit-and-fade, use mobility, conserve, win by attrition and humiliation. Decompensated Parker plants and trades. Against the Juggernaut-class opponent in the right state, this can produce a heroic outcome (Stern's "Nothing Can Stop the Juggernaut" arc is the canonical instance of stage-4 compulsion producing a moral victory through self-immolating persistence). Against an opponent calibrated to it — Kraven, who explicitly hunted the depleted version — the same pattern produces capture, near-death, and the kind of prolonged trauma the record shows.

**Romantic decompensation.** The intimacy-sabotage cycle has a specific shape. Under stage 1–2, he over-promises and under-shows-up. Under stage 3, he disappears physically and reappears with implausible explanations he no longer maintains the energy to construct properly. Under stage 4, he initiates the breach himself — picks a fight, makes a unilateral decision (often involving secrecy or self-sacrifice on the partner's behalf without consultation), and frames the resulting rupture as the partner's safety requiring it. The partner experiences this as withdrawal; he experiences it as protection; both are correct. The pattern repeated across the major romantic attachments is consistent enough to be diagnostic.

**Financial decompensation.** Idiosyncratic. He does not collapse financially under stress; he collapses *toward* financial precarity even when he has resources, because stability is incongruent with his self-concept. The Parker Industries arc — where he briefly inhabited Stark-coded affluence and competence — collapsed not from external defeat alone but from his own inability to sustain the frame. He returns to scraping by because scraping by is where he believes he belongs. This is a slow-motion failure mode rather than an acute decompensation; it operates as a constant downward pressure rather than an event.

**Identity-secrecy decompensation.** The compartmentalization is, at baseline, exceptional — six decades of operation with limited catastrophic exposure given the threat surface is itself remarkable. Decompensation here is **erosion rather than rupture** in most cases, with a single rupture event (2006) standing out. The erosion signature is the stage-2 slippage already described: residues, inconsistent cover stories, geographic implausibilities, lapses in tradecraft that he is normally fastidious about. Adversaries with patience and observational discipline have repeatedly deduced his identity from these slips; the record shows it is not a question of whether the inner circle of villains can deduce it under sustained surveillance, but of how often the deductions are suppressed, killed off, or magically erased.

**Mentorship decompensation.** A late-developed domain and the one in which he most reliably *recovers* function rather than losing it. Occupying the Ben-position for younger heroes (Miles primarily, the broader Spider-Family secondarily) is reparative; it interrupts the undoing loop by providing an alternative use for the protective drive. The failure mode here is overcorrection — he can become controlling or over-protective in ways that mirror, transposed, what he resented from authority figures in his own youth. This is a mild failure mode and self-correcting, because his self-awareness around the parallel is high.

---

## 6.5 RECOVERY ARCHITECTURE

For completeness: he does recover, repeatedly, from stage-5 events. The recovery is rarely complete — each stage-5 leaves residue, and the stack of unmetabolized losses grows — but the operational return to baseline is reliable. The conditions that produce recovery are the inverse of the conditions that produce collapse:

- **Resumption of witness.** A primary attachment figure returns and sees him. Often this is May; historically often MJ; latterly Miles or another Spider-Family member. The witnessing does not need to involve insight; presence is the active ingredient.
- **A clear external mission of finite scope.** Not the open-ended patrol load but a discrete problem with a definite end. Solving it provides a sublimation outlet that resolves rather than compounds.
- **Physiological reset.** Sleep, food, time without the mask. He resists this and requires it; intimates who insist on it across his objections are functionally providing medical care he will not seek.
- **Mentorship occasion.** Being asked for help by a younger hero in a way that requires him to model the function he cannot perform for himself. This is the most consistently effective intervention in the late record.

What the record does *not* show is recovery through clinical intervention, formal grief work, or any structured psychological treatment. The recovery architecture is entirely informal, relational, and contingent. **The single greatest gap in his protective ecosystem is the absence of any institutional safety net for the failure modes documented above.** A subject this consequential, sustaining this trauma load, with this stack of unresolved losses, is held together by the attention of perhaps four to six individuals and the occasional successful patrol. The system has worked for sixty years. The system's failures are documented above. The system's continuing function should not be confused with its adequacy.

---

*End of section. See §7 for Operational Profile and §8 for Adversary Modeling, including the specific exploitations of the failure architecture documented here by Osborn, Octavius, and Kraven respectively.*


## Trajectory & Forward Assessment

# 6. TRAJECTORY & FORWARD ASSESSMENT

*Forecast horizon: short (0–18 months operational), medium (2–7 years arc-scale), long (decade-plus, biographical). Probabilities are expressed qualitatively; the subject is a stable system perturbed at irregular intervals by external shocks, and his response to each shock is more predictable than the shocks themselves.*

---

## 6.1 The Operating Equilibrium He Is Currently In

To forecast the subject, one must first name the steady-state he has occupied for most of his adult life. It is not "happiness" and not "crisis"; it is a **low-amplitude, high-frequency oscillation around a setpoint of just-barely-sustainable distress**. The setpoint is held in place by four counter-acting forces:

1. **Compulsive prosocial action** (drives functional output upward; drains soma).
2. **Somatic self-neglect** (drains soma further; eventually forces collapse-and-reset).
3. **Intermittent intimacy** (provides short bursts of regulation; introduces new attachment-loss anxiety).
4. **Humor / intellectualization / sublimation** (smooths affect; prevents the system from breaking but also prevents it from being repaired).

This equilibrium is *meta-stable*. It can absorb significant perturbation — losses, betrayals, body-swaps, public exposures — and return to the setpoint within months. What it cannot do is improve on its own. There is no internal mechanism in the subject's behavioral repertoire that **bends the setpoint upward**. Every prior period of apparent flourishing in the record (the married years; the Parker Industries years; the brief stabilities under various writers) was destabilized not by an external villain but by the subject's own inability to tolerate sustained good fortune as compatible with his moral self-image. The forecast must therefore be read in two registers: what *will happen to* him, and what *he will do with* it.

---

## 6.2 Short Horizon (0–18 Months) — Operational

Across any given near-term window, the base rates of his behavior are extremely well-characterized and the file can project with high confidence:

- **Probability of a major identity-exposure event:** moderate. The compartmentalization has been catastrophically breached at least three times in the record (Civil War unmasking; the JMS-era May discovery; the post-Superior fallout). The subject's tradecraft has improved but his attachment behavior — the need to be *known* by intimates — works structurally against operational security. Expect at least one near-miss per 12-month cycle and a non-trivial chance of a successful breach by a sophisticated adversary every 3–4 years.
- **Probability of acute medical event requiring extended downtime:** high. Concussion-coded incidents are near-monthly; the mutation buffers but does not erase cumulative load. Within an 18-month window, expect at least one fracture-class injury, at least one toxicology event (Goblin formula, Lizard saliva, novel chemical), and a 30–50% chance of a hospitalization or comparable forced rest.
- **Probability of a romantic re-engagement or formalization:** moderate-to-high if a stable partner is present at window-start; moderate if not. He does not tolerate long romantic vacuum without seeking; the cycle of pursuit-and-sabotage is structural.
- **Probability of a mentorship-deepening event with a younger spider-coded figure:** very high. This is the most reparative behavior in his repertoire and the one he reaches for unprompted when in low mood; expect it to recur whenever his own affect dips.
- **Probability of a financial crisis:** high. He sabotages money the way he sabotages romance — at threshold. Predict at least one rent/job/eviction-tier event per cycle.

The short horizon, in short, is a known waveform. The dossier's forecasting value here is low because the subject's value is.

---

## 6.3 Medium Horizon (2–7 Years) — Arc-Scale Forks

This is where the forecast becomes interesting because it is where the subject's choices actually matter. The medium-horizon space is dominated by **a small number of high-leverage fork points**, each of which has been repeatedly visited in the record without resolution. Each fork can be projected with named pressure-vectors that would push him one way or the other.

### Fork A — The Mortality of May Parker

The single largest forecasting variable in the entire file. May is the load-bearing object of his original responsibility schema; her death (a final, definitive death — not a near-miss, not a reversal, not a Mephisto trade) would be the **largest characterological shock the subject has not yet had to metabolize at scale**. The Ben death created the schema; a May death would test whether the schema can survive the removal of its primary referent.

- **Catastrophe vector:** May dies under circumstances his moral logic can route to his own omission — a kidnapping by an identity-aware adversary, an attack he failed to predict, a slow illness during which he was patrolling. Predicted response: a 6–18 month decompensation into the deepest depressive episode of his life; passive-suicidal operational tempo (taking fights he expects to lose); withdrawal from intimate attachments to protect them from the curse he believes he carries; possible total identity-abandonment attempt that he cannot sustain past 60–90 days. The post-Superior, post-One More Day record shows he survives ego-death; he would survive this. He would not exit it the same person.
- **Growth vector:** May dies in a manner not routable to his omission — peaceful, of age, in a context where his presence was sufficient and his protection was not the relevant variable. Predicted response: acute grief but the possibility, for the first time, of **decoupling love from protection in his cognitive schema**. This is the only path the file can identify by which the originating distortion is metabolized rather than reinforced. Probability the universe delivers this version: low. Probability he allows himself to *receive* it as that version if delivered: lower still, without external scaffolding (see §6.5).

### Fork B — The Mary Jane Watson Question

The relationship is the file's most persistent attractor and the subject's most plausible vector toward sustained adult flourishing. The history is one of *near-misses with the conditions for stability* — the marriage worked; what destabilized it were external shocks (Mephisto trade) and internal sabotage (his inability to disclose pain, her resulting withdrawal, the loop). The forecast space:

- **Catastrophe vector:** MJ exits permanently into a stable life with another partner and child. Predicted response: outward grace, private grief, accelerated mentorship behavior (Ben-position for someone else's child becomes the substitute), incremental hardening of the belief that intimacy is foreclosed to him. He would not become bitter; he would become more *isolated under a friendlier surface*. This is the most likely outcome on current vectors and is the medium-horizon catastrophe that does not announce itself as a catastrophe.
- **Growth vector:** A reunion conducted with **disclosure as the operational principle** — that is, a version of the relationship in which he is required, as a condition of its continuation, to tell her when he is in pain. The historical pattern is that he cannot do this unprompted; it would have to be structured by her or by a third party. If it happened, the prediction is that within 2–3 years his baseline dysthymia would lift measurably and his rate of self-sabotaging operational choices would decline.

### Fork C — The Mentorship Saturation Point

The Spider-Family configuration is the most underappreciated structural development in the subject's adult life. The presence of Miles Morales and the broader Spider-coded community provides him, for the first time, with **a peer-group that does not require him to occupy the protector role exclusively** — they are protectors too, and several of them are willing to protect *him*. This is novel.

- **Catastrophe vector:** He fails to allow the reciprocity — continues to occupy the senior-mentor position exclusively, refuses to be mentored back, refuses to be carried when injured, refuses to disclose. This is the default trajectory and the file rates it as the most likely. Outcome: the community provides him real social benefit but does not transform the schema.
- **Growth vector:** A discrete event in which a younger spider-figure intervenes to *prevent his self-destruction*, in a manner he cannot deflect with humor — an explicit, named intervention. The file rates this as low-probability unprompted but high-leverage if it occurs. It would be the closest thing to therapy his social ecology can produce.

### Fork D — Institutional Re-engagement

The subject's relationship to institutions (SHIELD, Avengers, Stark-coded structures, Future Foundation, Horizon, the various incarnations of Parker Industries) is patterned: he engages, finds the institution morally inadequate at some threshold, defects, returns to street-level operation. The cycle has run at least five times.

- **Catastrophe vector:** A re-engagement under conditions that re-stage the Civil War wound — being asked to validate an authority structure whose ends he distrusts. Predicted response: another high-cost defection, another loss of resources, another return to precarity, with an incremental loss of capacity to trust institutional offers.
- **Growth vector:** A small-scale institutional position — laboratory, teaching, research — that uses the scientific drive without putting him in command of others' moral choices. He has tolerated this in the record (the high-school-teacher years, the various lab-tech configurations) and it has historically been the most stabilizing employment pattern. The file recommends, in any benevolent-intervention framing, that this is the institutional posture most likely to hold.

### Fork E — The Killing Line

He has not crossed it. The line is held by character architecture, not by external pressure. The medium-horizon forecast must include the question of what would force the test.

- **Catastrophe vector:** An adversary forces a trolley-problem at scale — a Goblin-coded figure with May or a child in immediate threat, and a single-shot lethal solution. The subject's stated position is that he will not cross the line; the *behavioral* record (the post-Gwen rage at Norman; the post-Kraven moments; the Superior period's residue) suggests he is closer to the line than his self-concept admits. If forced and he crossed, the file projects catastrophic identity collapse — not because the act would be unforgivable in the moral economy he inhabits but because **his self-concept is partially organized around having not crossed it**, and the collapse would be of the scaffolding rather than of the morality.
- **Growth vector:** A scenario in which the line is tested and he holds it *with full awareness that holding it has a cost he is paying knowingly* — rather than as a reflex. This would integrate the holding rather than leaving it as a brittle rule. Low probability without external scaffolding.

---

## 6.4 Long Horizon (Decade-Plus) — The Biographical Question

The long-horizon question is not what *happens to* him; it is what kind of older man he becomes. The file can specify several possible terminal trajectories with their preconditions.

**Trajectory L1 — The Ben Parker Completion.** He becomes, in late middle age, an effective Ben-position for a generation of younger figures: mentor, scientific resource, moral exemplar, with operational tempo gradually reduced. He retires the mask incrementally rather than catastrophically. The schema is not cured but is *enacted in its reparative form* — he is now the uncle, and the uncle survives, and the survival itself rewrites the original lesson at a level his cognitive defenses cannot block. Preconditions: a stable enough intimate life that he does not need patrol for regulation; a recognized successor or successors; a discrete decision (rather than a forced retirement). Probability: moderate if Forks A, B, and C resolve toward growth; low otherwise.

**Trajectory L2 — The Operator Who Never Stops.** He patrols into his sixties and seventies with declining physical capacity buffered by experience and tradecraft, sustained by a refusal to allow the role to lapse. He becomes the man on the rooftop in all weather. He is admired and largely alone. He dies on patrol, eventually, in a fight he could have walked away from. The schema completes itself by killing him in the role. Probability: moderate; this is the default if no fork resolves toward growth.

**Trajectory L3 — The Catastrophic Decompensation.** A sufficiently large unmetabolized loss (Fork A in the catastrophe form, or a compound of A and B) overwhelms the defenses. He does not become a villain — the character architecture forbids it — but he becomes a recluse, a withdrawn figure whose continuing existence in the city is itself a kind of haunting. The wit goes quiet. The science continues, privately. Probability: low-to-moderate; the defensive structure is strong but not infinitely so.

**Trajectory L4 — The Integrated Older Man.** The least likely and most desirable. Some combination of sustained partnership, mentorship reciprocity, and a discrete reparative event (most plausibly: surviving a loss without routing it to his own omission) produces a late-life subject who carries the original wound as *biography* rather than as ongoing injury. He is still funny, still anxious in the old places, still scientifically restless; but the baseline dysthymia lifts, the operational tempo modulates to sustainable levels, and the protective curse-belief loosens enough that he allows himself to be loved without flinching. Probability: low without external scaffolding; modest with it.

---

## 6.5 What Would Push Him Toward Growth

The file's central forecasting claim is that the subject **cannot self-correct from within his current defensive structure**. The defenses are too effective at maintaining the setpoint. Growth requires inputs the system would not generate on its own:

1. **A relationship in which disclosure is structurally required, not optional.** He will not disclose unprompted; he will disclose if disclosure is the price of the relationship and the relationship is one he cannot bear to lose. MJ historically has been the only figure plausibly capable of this; a sufficiently insistent younger spider-figure or a peer-hero in a structured mentorship-back role could approximate it.
2. **A loss he cannot route to omission.** The schema requires a causal pathway to his own failure; a loss that genuinely offers no such pathway, *experienced as such*, would constitute the first piece of evidence against the schema that the schema cannot metabolize. This is rare because he is creative about routing.
3. **A success he is required to inhabit.** Sustained stability — financial, romantic, vocational — that he is not allowed to sabotage because the costs of sabotage are borne by dependents he cannot betray. The mentorship configuration provides a weak version of this; a more robust version would be transformative.
4. **Permission, from a figure whose authority he accepts, to rest.** He has never received this in the record. May has tried; MJ has tried; the closest historical analog is the brief moments in which a peer he respects has told him explicitly to stand down and he has, momentarily, complied. A sustained version — a standing instruction from a respected source that rest is a duty co-equal with patrol — could shift the somatic neglect pattern measurably.
5. **An encounter with his own conscience that is not punitive.** The defining feature of his moral self-relation is its asymmetry: he extends compassion outward and withholds it from himself. Any intervention — therapeutic, spiritual, or relational — that successfully introduced self-compassion as a permitted move would be the largest single corrective the file can identify.

---

## 6.6 What Would Push Him Toward Catastrophe

Symmetrically:

1. **A loss of May Parker routable to omission** (Fork A, catastrophe form).
2. **A definitive exit of MJ** combined with the foreclosure of the mentorship community (a compound Fork B–C catastrophe).
3. **A forced crossing of the killing line** under conditions he cannot frame as anything other than his own choice.
4. **A second symbiote-class loss of agency** — any extended period in which his body acts without his consent — would compound the unmetabolized residue from the first such episode and the Superior occupation, and could destabilize the volitional-control schema that currently holds.
5. **A public, institutional, irreversible identity exposure** of a kind that cannot be retconned or magicked away — that placed his intimates in permanent danger. The Civil War wound was partially anesthetized by the One More Day reset; a version that *stayed* would test the limits.
6. **A discovery that one of his foundational moral premises was false** — for instance, that Ben's death was not preventable by his action, or that the responsibility framework he has built his life on was, in its origin, a misreading. The file rates this as paradoxically high-risk: the schema is so load-bearing that its disconfirmation could be more destabilizing than its confirmation.

---

## 6.7 Open Questions the File Cannot Yet Resolve

- **The mutation's long-term endocrine and neurological trajectory.** No longitudinal medical data exist. Whether the accelerated healing fully compensates for cumulative TBI, repeated toxin exposure, and chronic sleep deprivation across a 60-year operational career is an empirical question that will be answered, one way or the other, by his sixties.
- **The permanence of the post-Superior residue.** Whether the Octavius occupation left durable changes — in tradecraft, in willingness to delegate, in subtle alterations of strategic style — or whether the apparent changes have fully reverted to baseline. The record is ambiguous and the subject does not introspect on it publicly.
- **The status of the totemic framing.** Whether the JMS-era spider-totem mythology is a real ontological feature of his existence or a metaphor he was briefly subjected to. If real, it implies a class of adversary (Morlun-coded inheritors) that will recur on a long cycle and that he is structurally vulnerable to in ways the file cannot fully characterize.
- **The succession question.** Whether the Spider-Family configuration is a transitional structure toward an eventual handoff or a stable adult-life configuration in which the role is distributed permanently. His behavior is consistent with both readings.
- **The disclosure ceiling.** Whether there exists any relational configuration in which he would voluntarily disclose the full extent of his pain to another human. The historical record says no; the forecast must hold the question open because the answer determines which long-horizon trajectory obtains.

---

## 6.8 Summative Forecast

The subject is, in forecasting terms, a **highly stable system with a low ceiling and a moderately resilient floor**. He will not become a villain; he will not become catatonic; he will not, on current trajectories, become well. The most likely terminal trajectory is **L2 — the operator who does not stop** — punctuated by episodic decompensations that he recovers from with diminishing speed as the soma accumulates load. The most desirable trajectory, **L4**, is achievable but requires inputs his defensive structure will not generate unprompted; it depends almost entirely on whether the people who love him develop the will and the skill to insist on disclosure, rest, and the receipt of care as non-negotiable terms of their relationships with him.

The file's operational recommendation to any benevolent observer with influence over his social ecology is narrow and specific: do not try to fix the schema. The schema is the man. Instead, **scaffold the conditions under which the schema's reparative enactment becomes more available than its punitive enactment** — protect the mentorship configurations, support the partnership when it is present, make explicit the permission to rest, and, when a loss arrives that offers no honest pathway to his own omission, *help him see that this is what it is* before his cognitive machinery routes it back to the original wound.

He has carried the weight for sixty years. Whether he carries it for the next thirty as injury or as biography is, in the file's assessment, the only question that matters.
